  declare ~tbl_rate__decay

  set_control_par(get_ui_id(%tbl_int2), $CONTROL_PAR_PARENT_PANEL, get_ui_id($UI_vibrato))
  $tbl_rate__curve := $sli_envRateCurve
  ~tbl_rate__attack_point := pow(10.0, (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)) + ((((int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.510000000000000) - 0.0) / (int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0.0)) * ((log(0.056000000000000) / log(10.0)) - (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)))))
  $tbl_rate__release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.750000000000000)
  ~tbl_rate__attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_envRateAttack)) - 0.0) * (~tbl_rate__attack_point - 1.500000000000000)) / 1000000.0) + 1.500000000000000
  $tbl_rate__hold := (($sli_envRateHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.150000000000000) - 0)) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_envRateDecay)) - 0.0) * 14200.0) / 1000000.0) + 800.0
  $tbl_rate__sustain := (($sli_envRateSustain - 0) * 1000) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0.0) * 39200.0) / 1000000.0) + 800.0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := real_to_int(exp(~tbl_rate__attack * int_to_real($i)))
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1.0 / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.0) * 10.990000000000000) / 14200.0) + 0.010000000000000))) * ~tbl_rate__decay) - ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.0) * 200.0) / 14200.0) + 0.0))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := (((%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] - 0) * (1000 - $tbl_rate__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_rate__sustain
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1.0 / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.0) * 4.990000000000000) / 14200.0) + 0.010000000000000))) * ~tbl_rate__release) - ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.0) * 300.0) / 14200.0) + 0.0))
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_rate__attack_idx := search(%tbl_rate__expCurve, 1000)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__linCurve[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real($i) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($tbl_rate__attack_idx) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
    %tbl_rate__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[((($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right(($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31))) - ($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_rate__curve < 500000)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.0) * -1.0) / 500000.0) + 1.0)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.0) * 1.0) / 500000.0) + 0.0))
    else
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.0) * -1.0) / 500000.0) + 1.0)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__logCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.0) * 1.0) / 500000.0) + 0.0))
    end if
    if($i > ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold))
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] - 0) * (real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$tbl_rate__release_idx]) - 0)) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_rate__release_idx)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_rate__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= ($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate1[$i] := (((((real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.880000000000000) - 0)) / 1000
    %tbl_rate2[$i] := %tbl_rate1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_int__curve := $sli_envIntCurve
  ~tbl_int__attack_point := pow(10.0, (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)) + ((((int_to_real($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.510000000000000) - 0.0) / (int_to_real($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0.0)) * ((log(0.056000000000000) / log(10.0)) - (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)))))
  $tbl_int__release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.750000000000000)
  ~tbl_int__attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_envIntAttack)) - 0.0) * (~tbl_int__attack_point - 1.500000000000000)) / 1000000.0) + 1.500000000000000
  $tbl_int__hold := (($sli_envIntHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.150000000000000) - 0)) / 1000000
  ~tbl_int__decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_envIntDecay)) - 0.0) * 14200.0) / 1000000.0) + 800.0
  $tbl_int__sustain := (($sli_envIntSustain - 0) * 1000) / 1000000
  ~tbl_int__release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0.0) * 39200.0) / 1000000.0) + 800.0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__expCurve[$i] := real_to_int(exp(~tbl_int__attack * int_to_real($i)))
    %tbl_int__expCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_int__expCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__expCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_int__expCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1.0 / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_int__decay - 800.0) * 10.990000000000000) / 14200.0) + 0.010000000000000))) * ~tbl_int__decay) - ((((~tbl_int__decay - 800.0) * 200.0) / 14200.0) + 0.0))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := (((%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] - 0) * (1000 - $tbl_int__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_int__sustain
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1.0 / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_int__release - 800.0) * 4.990000000000000) / 14200.0) + 0.010000000000000))) * ~tbl_int__release) - ((((~tbl_int__release - 800.0) * 300.0) / 14200.0) + 0.0))
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_int__attack_idx := search(%tbl_int__expCurve, 1000)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__linCurve[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real($i) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($tbl_int__attack_idx) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
    %tbl_int__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[((($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right(($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31))) - ($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_int__curve < 500000)
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_int__expCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 0.0) * -1.0) / 500000.0) + 1.0)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_int__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 0.0) * 1.0) / 500000.0) + 0.0))
    else
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_int__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 500000.0) * -1.0) / 500000.0) + 1.0)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_int__logCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 500000.0) * 1.0) / 500000.0) + 0.0))
    end if
    if($i > ($tbl_int__attack_idx + $tbl_int__hold))
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i - ($tbl_int__attack_idx + $tbl_int__hold)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] - 0) * (real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$tbl_int__release_idx]) - 0)) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_int__release_idx)
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_int__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= ($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
    %tbl_int1[$i] := (((((real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.880000000000000) - 0)) / 1000
    %tbl_int2[$i] := %tbl_int1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while

    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_legatoList), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoList])

      $loc_12 := 0
      $loc_13 := 0

        !legatoList__trans_file_names[$loc_12] := !file_names_master[$loc_12]
        %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$loc_12] := %zone_ids_master[$loc_12]
        %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_12] := 0
        !legatoList__intervals[$loc_12] := ""
        !legatoList__comments[$loc_12] := ""
        inc($loc_12)
      end while
      $loc_12 := 0
      while($loc_12 <= ($NUM_TRANS_SAMPLES_PLAYED - 1)) 
        $loc_13 := search(%zone_ids_master, %trans_zone_ids[$loc_12])
        if($loc_13 # -1)
          %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_13] := %marked_samples[$loc_12]
          !legatoList__intervals[$loc_13] := !intervals[$loc_12]
          !legatoList__comments[$loc_13] := !sample_comments[$loc_12]
        end if
        inc($loc_12)
      end while
      $loc_11 := 0
      $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD := $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS
      $NUM_PRESETS := search(%zone_ids_master, - 1)
      $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS := $NUM_PRESETS
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_presetcount), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS & "/" & $NUM_PRESETS)
      if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD # $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
        $loc_11 := 0
        while($loc_11 <= (num_elements(%legatoList__end_of_list) - 1)) 
          %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := - 1
          if($loc_11 < $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
            %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := 1
          end if
          inc($loc_11)
        end while
      end if
      $scroll__up := real_to_int((((~scroll__realup - 0.0) * (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD - 12) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
      if($element__idx # -1)
        %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 1
        if(not in_range($element__idx, $scroll__up, $scroll__up + 12))
          $scroll__up := $element__idx - 5
        end if
        if(($element__idx - 2) <= $scroll__up)
          $scroll__up := $element__idx - 2
        else
          if(($element__idx + 2) > (($scroll__up + 12) - 1))
            $scroll__up := ($element__idx + 2) - 11
          end if
        end if
        $scroll__up := ($scroll__up * (1 + (sh_right(($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - $scroll__up, 31) .or. sh_right($scroll__up - 0, 31)))) - (($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) * sh_right(($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - $scroll__up, 31))
      end if
      $sli_scrollbar := 1000000 - ((1000000 / ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12)) * $scroll__up)
      $i := 0
      while($i <= 11) 
        set_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%btn_element_completed[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%btn_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(%btn_element_played[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
        set_control_par_str(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !legatoList__trans_file_names[$i + $scroll__up])
        set_control_par_str(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$i + $scroll__up])
        set_control_par_str(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !legatoList__intervals[$i + $scroll__up])
        set_control_par_str(!txt_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !legatoList__comments[$i + $scroll__up])
        set_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %btn_elements_onoff[$i + $scroll__up])
        set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
        set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
        set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
        set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
        set_control_par(%btn_element_completed[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %completed_elements[$i + $scroll__up])
        set_control_par(%btn_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %legatoList__marked_elements[$i + $scroll__up])
        set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%legatoList__marked_elements[$i + $scroll__up]])

          set_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
          set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
          set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
          set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
          set_control_par(%btn_element_completed[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
          set_control_par(%btn_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
          set_control_par(%btn_element_played[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
          set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
        end if

      end while
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + ((245 - $handle_size) - (($sli_scrollbar * (245 - $handle_size)) / 1000000)))
      if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS > 12)
        $sli_scrollbar := 1000000 - ((1000000 / ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12)) * $scroll__up)

function load__array
  $i := $preset_idx__BODY
  while($i <= 99) 
    if(%uiControls[$i - $preset_idx__BODY] # 0)
      set_control_par(%uiControls[$i - $preset_idx__BODY], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %vibrato_preset[$i])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0], get_ui_id($sli_envRateCurve), %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "ENV_AHDSR"), - 1)
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_rate__curve := $sli_envRateCurve
  ~tbl_rate__attack_point := pow(10.0, (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)) + ((((int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.510000000000000) - 0.0) / (int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0.0)) * ((log(0.056000000000000) / log(10.0)) - (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)))))
  $tbl_rate__release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.750000000000000)
  ~tbl_rate__attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_envRateAttack)) - 0.0) * (~tbl_rate__attack_point - 1.500000000000000)) / 1000000.0) + 1.500000000000000
  $tbl_rate__hold := (($sli_envRateHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.150000000000000) - 0)) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_envRateDecay)) - 0.0) * 14200.0) / 1000000.0) + 800.0
  $tbl_rate__sustain := (($sli_envRateSustain - 0) * 1000) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0.0) * 39200.0) / 1000000.0) + 800.0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := real_to_int(exp(~tbl_rate__attack * int_to_real($i)))
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1.0 / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.0) * 10.990000000000000) / 14200.0) + 0.010000000000000))) * ~tbl_rate__decay) - ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.0) * 200.0) / 14200.0) + 0.0))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := (((%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] - 0) * (1000 - $tbl_rate__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_rate__sustain
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1.0 / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.0) * 4.990000000000000) / 14200.0) + 0.010000000000000))) * ~tbl_rate__release) - ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.0) * 300.0) / 14200.0) + 0.0))
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_rate__attack_idx := search(%tbl_rate__expCurve, 1000)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__linCurve[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real($i) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($tbl_rate__attack_idx) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
    %tbl_rate__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[((($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right(($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31))) - ($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_rate__curve < 500000)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.0) * -1.0) / 500000.0) + 1.0)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.0) * 1.0) / 500000.0) + 0.0))
    else
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.0) * -1.0) / 500000.0) + 1.0)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__logCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.0) * 1.0) / 500000.0) + 0.0))
    end if
    if($i > ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold))
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] - 0) * (real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$tbl_rate__release_idx]) - 0)) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_rate__release_idx)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_rate__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= ($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate1[$i] := (((((real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.880000000000000) - 0)) / 1000
    %tbl_rate2[$i] := %tbl_rate1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[1], get_ui_id($sli_envRateAttack), %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "ENV_AHDSR"), - 1)
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_rate__curve := $sli_envRateCurve
  ~tbl_rate__attack_point := pow(10.0, (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)) + ((((int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.510000000000000) - 0.0) / (int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0.0)) * ((log(0.056000000000000) / log(10.0)) - (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)))))
  $tbl_rate__release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.750000000000000)
  ~tbl_rate__attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_envRateAttack)) - 0.0) * (~tbl_rate__attack_point - 1.500000000000000)) / 1000000.0) + 1.500000000000000
  $tbl_rate__hold := (($sli_envRateHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.150000000000000) - 0)) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_envRateDecay)) - 0.0) * 14200.0) / 1000000.0) + 800.0
  $tbl_rate__sustain := (($sli_envRateSustain - 0) * 1000) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0.0) * 39200.0) / 1000000.0) + 800.0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := real_to_int(exp(~tbl_rate__attack * int_to_real($i)))
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1.0 / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.0) * 10.990000000000000) / 14200.0) + 0.010000000000000))) * ~tbl_rate__decay) - ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.0) * 200.0) / 14200.0) + 0.0))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := (((%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] - 0) * (1000 - $tbl_rate__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_rate__sustain
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1.0 / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.0) * 4.990000000000000) / 14200.0) + 0.010000000000000))) * ~tbl_rate__release) - ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.0) * 300.0) / 14200.0) + 0.0))
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_rate__attack_idx := search(%tbl_rate__expCurve, 1000)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__linCurve[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real($i) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($tbl_rate__attack_idx) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
    %tbl_rate__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[((($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right(($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31))) - ($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_rate__curve < 500000)

function save__preset
  $load_id := load_array_str(%vibrato_preset, @base_path & @txt_presetName & ".nka")
  wait_async(load_array_str(%vibrato_preset, @base_path & @txt_presetName & ".nka"))
  if($load_id # -1)
    %vibPresetCount[$presetCount] := 1
    !vibPresetNames[$presetCount] := @txt_presetName
    save__resource_arrays
    $mnu_preset := $presetCount
    $presetCount := ((($presetCount + 1) * (1 + (sh_right(100 - ($presetCount + 1), 31) .or. sh_right(($presetCount + 1) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(($presetCount + 1) - 0, 31))) - (100 * sh_right(100 - ($presetCount + 1), 31))
    $preset_scan := $TRUE
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_scanPresets), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "alpha")
  end if
  %vibrato_preset[$preset_idx__DELETED] := $FALSE
  $i := $preset_idx__BODY
  while($i <= 99) 
    if(%uiControls[$i - $preset_idx__BODY] # 0)
      %vibrato_preset[$i] := get_control_par(%uiControls[$i - $preset_idx__BODY], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  save_array_str(%vibrato_preset, @base_path & @txt_presetName & ".nka")
  call update__preset__menu
end function
function update__lfoFadeIn
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_LFO_DELAY, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_lfoFadeIn)) - 0.0) * 900000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0), %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), - 1)
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update__lfoFreq
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_INTMOD_FREQUENCY, real_to_int((((int_to_real(((($sli_lfoFreq + %lfoRandValues[$event_note]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - ($sli_lfoFreq + %lfoRandValues[$event_note]), 31) .or. sh_right(($sli_lfoFreq + %lfoRandValues[$event_note]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(($sli_lfoFreq + %lfoRandValues[$event_note]) - 0, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - ($sli_lfoFreq + %lfoRandValues[$event_note]), 31))) - 0.0) * 200000.0) / 1000000.0) + 450000.0), %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), - 1)
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update__pitchModulation
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_MOD_TARGET_INTENSITY, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_pitchModulation)) - 0.0) * 200000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0), %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), find_target(%vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), "LFO_MULTI D" & "_PITCH"))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $current_pitchModulation := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_pitchModulation)) - 0.0) * 200000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
end function
function update__cc_vibrato
  set_controller(101, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_vibrato)) - 0.0) * 127.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0))
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_MOD_TARGET_INTENSITY, get_ui_id($sli_vibrato), %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), find_target(%vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), "LFO_MULTI D" & "_EQ_GAIN_1"))
    set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_MOD_TARGET_INTENSITY, (($sli_vibrato - 0) * ($current_pitchModulation - 0)) / 1000000, %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), find_target(%vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), "LFO_MULTI D" & "_PITCH"))
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update__preset_button_focus
  if($element__idx # -1)
    %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 1
    if(not in_range($element__idx, $scroll__up, $scroll__up + 12))
      $scroll__up := $element__idx - 5
    end if
    if(($element__idx - 2) <= $scroll__up)
      $scroll__up := $element__idx - 2
    else
      if(($element__idx + 2) > (($scroll__up + 12) - 1))
        $scroll__up := ($element__idx + 2) - 11
      end if
    end if
    $scroll__up := ($scroll__up * (1 + (sh_right(($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - $scroll__up, 31) .or. sh_right($scroll__up - 0, 31)))) - (($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) * sh_right(($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - $scroll__up, 31))
  end if
end function
function update__scrollbar
  $sli_scrollbar := 1000000 - ((1000000 / ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12)) * $scroll__up)
end function
function update__scrollarea
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 11) 
    set_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(%btn_element_completed[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(%btn_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(%btn_element_played[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
    set_control_par_str(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !legatoList__trans_file_names[$i + $scroll__up])
    set_control_par_str(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$i + $scroll__up])
    set_control_par_str(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !legatoList__intervals[$i + $scroll__up])
    set_control_par_str(!txt_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !legatoList__comments[$i + $scroll__up])
    set_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %btn_elements_onoff[$i + $scroll__up])
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
    set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
    set_control_par(%btn_element_completed[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %completed_elements[$i + $scroll__up])
    set_control_par(%btn_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %legatoList__marked_elements[$i + $scroll__up])
    set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[%legatoList__marked_elements[$i + $scroll__up]])
    if(%legatoList__end_of_list[$i + $scroll__up] = -1)
      set_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%btn_element_completed[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%btn_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(%btn_element_played[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + ((245 - $handle_size) - (($sli_scrollbar * (245 - $handle_size)) / 1000000)))
end function
function load__preset
  wait_async(load_array_str(%vibrato_preset, @base_path & !vibPresetNames[$mnu_preset] & ".nka"))
  call load__array
end function
function get__presetCount
  $presetCount := search(%vibPresetCount, 0)
  $presetCount := (($presetCount * (1 + (sh_right(100 - $presetCount, 31) .or. sh_right($presetCount - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right($presetCount - 0, 31))) - (100 * sh_right(100 - $presetCount, 31))
end function
function update__eqGain
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_GAIN1, get_ui_id($sli_eqGain), %vibrato_groups[$i], 5, 1)
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update__gainModulation
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_LFO_SINE, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_gainModulation)) - 0.0) * 500000.0) / 1000000.0) + 500000.0), %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "LFO_MULTI D"), - 1)
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function save__completed_array
  save_array_str(%completed_elements, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "completed_elements.nka")
end function
function update__fadeOutTrans
  %trans_fadeOut_time[$trans_idx] := $sli_fadeOutTrans
  ~current_fadeInTime := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_fadeOutTrans)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_fadeOutTrans), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, real_to_int(~current_fadeInTime) & " ms")
  ~real := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_fadeOutTrans)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fadeOutCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~real * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~real * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~real * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~real * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~real * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fadeOutCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
end function
function update__sampleComment
  if(%marked_samples[$trans_idx] = 0)
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(@txt_sampleComment), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "Leave a comment and hit [Enter]")
  else
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(@txt_sampleComment), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !sample_comments[$trans_idx])
  end if
  set_control_par(get_ui_id(@txt_sampleComment), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_markSample])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_sampleCommentBG), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_markSample])
end function
function update__lfoRand
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%lfoRandValues) - 1)) 
    %lfoRandValues[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%randNoteValues[$i]) - -500.0) * (int_to_real($sli_lfoRand / 10) - - int_to_real($sli_lfoRand / 10))) / 1000.0) + - int_to_real($sli_lfoRand / 10))
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update__intEnv
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_MOD_TARGET_INTENSITY, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_intEnv)) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0), %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "ENV_AHDSR2"), find_target(%vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "ENV_AHDSR2"), "ENV_AHDSR2" & "_INTENSITY"))
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function update__preset__menu
  if($presetCount = 0)
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(@txt_presetName), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "EMPTY PRESET")
  else
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(@txt_presetName), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !vibPresetNames[get_control_par(get_ui_id($mnu_preset), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)])
  end if
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 99) 
    if($i < $presetCount)
      set_menu_item_str(get_ui_id($mnu_preset), $i, !vibPresetNames[$i])
      set_menu_item_visibility(get_ui_id($mnu_preset), $i, $TRUE)
    else
      set_menu_item_visibility(get_ui_id($mnu_preset), $i, $FALSE)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
end function

end function
function update__fadeInSus
  %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx] := $sli_fadeInSus
  ~current_fadeInTime := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_fadeInSus)) - 0.0) * 500.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_fadeInSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, real_to_int(~current_fadeInTime) & " ms")
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_waitTime), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~current_fadeInTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~current_fadeInTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~current_fadeInTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~current_fadeInTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~current_fadeInTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
end function

end function

function update__waitSus
  %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx] := $sli_waitSus
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_waitSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_waitSus)) - 0.0) * 500.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0) & " ms")
  ~current_fadeInTime := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_fadeInSus)) - 0.0) * 500.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_waitTime), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~current_fadeInTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~current_fadeInTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~current_fadeInTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~current_fadeInTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~current_fadeInTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  ~current_waitTime := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_waitSus)) - 0.0) * 500.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_waitTime), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + 2) + real_to_int(((((~current_waitTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_waitTime), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, (555 - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_waitTime), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X)) - 2)
end function
function save__resource_arrays
  save_array(!vibPresetNames, 1)
  save_array(%vibPresetCount, 1)
end function
function load__arrays
  wait_async(load_array_str(!trans_file_names, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "trans_file_names.nka"))
  wait_async(load_array_str(!intervals, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "intervals.nka"))
  wait_async(load_array_str(%trans_zone_ids, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "trans_zone_ids.nka"))
  wait_async(load_array_str(%trans_zone_start, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "trans_zone_start.nka"))
  wait_async(load_array_str(%trans_event_volume, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "trans_event_volume.nka"))
  wait_async(load_array_str(%trans_wait_time, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "trans_wait_time.nka"))
  wait_async(load_array_str(%trans_fadeIn_time, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "trans_fadeIn_time.nka"))
  wait_async(load_array_str(%trans_fadeOut_time, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "trans_fadeOut_time.nka"))
  wait_async(load_array_str(%sus_release_time, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "sus_release_time.nka"))
  wait_async(load_array_str(%sus_fadeIn_time, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "sus_fadeIn_time.nka"))
  wait_async(load_array_str(%marked_samples, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "marked_samples.nka"))
  wait_async(load_array_str(!sample_comments, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "sample_comments.nka"))
  wait_async(load_array_str(!file_names_master, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "file_names_master.nka"))
  wait_async(load_array_str(%zone_ids_master, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "zone_ids_master.nka"))
  wait_async(load_array_str(%completed_elements, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "completed_elements.nka"))
  init__arrays
end function
function update__zoneVolume
  %trans_event_volume[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_volume)) - 0.0) * 20000.0) / 1000000.0) + -10000.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_volume), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (int_to_real(real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_volume)) - 0.0) * 20000.0) / 1000000.0) + -10000.0) / 10) / 100.0) & " dB")
end function
function update__cc_expression
  set_controller(111, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_expression)) - 0.0) * 127.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0))
end function
function apply__forall__settings
  $slider := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_samplestart)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real($max_samplestart * 1000) - 0.0)) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  $ii := ((real_to_int((int_to_real($slider) / 1000000.0) * 48000.0) * (1 + (sh_right($sample_end - real_to_int((int_to_real($slider) / 1000000.0) * 48000.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int((int_to_real($slider) / 1000000.0) * 48000.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int((int_to_real($slider) / 1000000.0) * 48000.0) - 0, 31))) - ($sample_end * sh_right($sample_end - real_to_int((int_to_real($slider) / 1000000.0) * 48000.0), 31))
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 1999) 
    if($i # $trans_idx)
      %sus_release_time[$i] := ((((%sus_release_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_releaseSus) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0) * $btn_check_releaseSus)) * (1 + (sh_right(real_to_int(1000.0) - ((%sus_release_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_releaseSus) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0) * $btn_check_releaseSus)), 31) .or. sh_right(((%sus_release_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_releaseSus) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0) * $btn_check_releaseSus)) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(((%sus_release_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_releaseSus) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0) * $btn_check_releaseSus)) - 0, 31))) - (real_to_int(1000.0) * sh_right(real_to_int(1000.0) - ((%sus_release_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_releaseSus) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0) * $btn_check_releaseSus)), 31))
      %trans_zone_start[$i] := ((((%trans_zone_start[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_samplestart) - 1, 31))) + ($ii * $btn_check_samplestart)) * (1 + (sh_right(real_to_int(((int_to_real($max_samplestart) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) * 48000.0) - ((%trans_zone_start[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_samplestart) - 1, 31))) + ($ii * $btn_check_samplestart)), 31) .or. sh_right(((%trans_zone_start[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_samplestart) - 1, 31))) + ($ii * $btn_check_samplestart)) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(((%trans_zone_start[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_samplestart) - 1, 31))) + ($ii * $btn_check_samplestart)) - 0, 31))) - (real_to_int(((int_to_real($max_samplestart) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) * 48000.0) * sh_right(real_to_int(((int_to_real($max_samplestart) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) * 48000.0) - ((%trans_zone_start[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_samplestart) - 1, 31))) + ($ii * $btn_check_samplestart)), 31))
      %trans_event_volume[$i] := ((((%trans_event_volume[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_volume) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_volume)) - 0.0) * 20000.0) / 1000000.0) + -10000.0) * $btn_check_volume)) * (1 + (sh_right(10000 - ((%trans_event_volume[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_volume) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_volume)) - 0.0) * 20000.0) / 1000000.0) + -10000.0) * $btn_check_volume)), 31) .or. sh_right(((%trans_event_volume[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_volume) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_volume)) - 0.0) * 20000.0) / 1000000.0) + -10000.0) * $btn_check_volume)) - -10000, 31)))) - (-10000 * sh_right(((%trans_event_volume[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_volume) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_volume)) - 0.0) * 20000.0) / 1000000.0) + -10000.0) * $btn_check_volume)) - -10000, 31))) - (10000 * sh_right(10000 - ((%trans_event_volume[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_volume) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_volume)) - 0.0) * 20000.0) / 1000000.0) + -10000.0) * $btn_check_volume)), 31))
      %trans_wait_time[$i] := ((((%trans_wait_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_waitSus) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_waitSus * $btn_check_waitSus)) * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - ((%trans_wait_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_waitSus) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_waitSus * $btn_check_waitSus)), 31) .or. sh_right(((%trans_wait_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_waitSus) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_waitSus * $btn_check_waitSus)) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(((%trans_wait_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_waitSus) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_waitSus * $btn_check_waitSus)) - 0, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - ((%trans_wait_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_waitSus) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_waitSus * $btn_check_waitSus)), 31))
      %sus_fadeIn_time[$i] := ((((%sus_fadeIn_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeInSus) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_fadeInSus * $btn_check_fadeInSus)) * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - ((%sus_fadeIn_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeInSus) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_fadeInSus * $btn_check_fadeInSus)), 31) .or. sh_right(((%sus_fadeIn_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeInSus) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_fadeInSus * $btn_check_fadeInSus)) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(((%sus_fadeIn_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeInSus) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_fadeInSus * $btn_check_fadeInSus)) - 0, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - ((%sus_fadeIn_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeInSus) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_fadeInSus * $btn_check_fadeInSus)), 31))
      %trans_fadeIn_time[$i] := ((((%trans_fadeIn_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeInTrans) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_fadeInTrans * $btn_check_fadeInTrans)) * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - ((%trans_fadeIn_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeInTrans) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_fadeInTrans * $btn_check_fadeInTrans)), 31) .or. sh_right(((%trans_fadeIn_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeInTrans) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_fadeInTrans * $btn_check_fadeInTrans)) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(((%trans_fadeIn_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeInTrans) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_fadeInTrans * $btn_check_fadeInTrans)) - 0, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - ((%trans_fadeIn_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeInTrans) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_fadeInTrans * $btn_check_fadeInTrans)), 31))
      %trans_fadeOut_time[$i] := ((((%trans_fadeOut_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeOutTrans) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_fadeOutTrans * $btn_check_fadeOutTrans)) * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - ((%trans_fadeOut_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeOutTrans) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_fadeOutTrans * $btn_check_fadeOutTrans)), 31) .or. sh_right(((%trans_fadeOut_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeOutTrans) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_fadeOutTrans * $btn_check_fadeOutTrans)) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(((%trans_fadeOut_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeOutTrans) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_fadeOutTrans * $btn_check_fadeOutTrans)) - 0, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - ((%trans_fadeOut_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeOutTrans) - 1, 31))) + ($sli_fadeOutTrans * $btn_check_fadeOutTrans)), 31))
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function save__arrays
  %async_ids[0] := save_array_str(!trans_file_names, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "trans_file_names.nka")
  %async_ids[1] := save_array_str(!intervals, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "intervals.nka")
  %async_ids[2] := save_array_str(%trans_zone_ids, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "trans_zone_ids.nka")
  %async_ids[3] := save_array_str(%trans_event_volume, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "trans_event_volume.nka")
  %async_ids[4] := save_array_str(%trans_zone_start, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "trans_zone_start.nka")
  %async_ids[5] := save_array_str(%trans_wait_time, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "trans_wait_time.nka")
  %async_ids[6] := save_array_str(%sus_release_time, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "sus_release_time.nka")
  %async_ids[7] := save_array_str(%sus_fadeIn_time, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "sus_fadeIn_time.nka")
  %async_ids[8] := save_array_str(%marked_samples, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "marked_samples.nka")
  %async_ids[9] := save_array_str(!sample_comments, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "sample_comments.nka")
  %async_ids[10] := save_array_str(%trans_fadeIn_time, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "trans_fadeIn_time.nka")
  %async_ids[11] := save_array_str(%trans_fadeOut_time, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "trans_fadeOut_time.nka")
  %async_ids[12] := save_array_str(%completed_elements, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "completed_elements.nka")
end function
function play_trans_sample
  $play_id := play_note($play_event, $play_velo, real_to_int((int_to_real(%trans_zone_start[$trans_idx]) / 48000.0) * 1000000.0), - 1)
  set_event_par_arr($play_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
  set_event_par_arr($play_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $current_trans_group)
  set_event_par_arr($play_id, $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, get_ui_id($sli_fadeInTrans), 3)
  set_event_par_arr($play_id, $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, get_ui_id($sli_fadeOutTrans), 5)
  change_vol($play_id, %trans_event_volume[$trans_idx], 0)
end function
function scan__samples
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_sModInd), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fadeInCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fadeOutCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_waitTime), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 1999) 
    %zone_ids_master[$i] := - 1
    !file_names_master[$i] := ""
    inc($i)
  end while
  $u := 0
  while($u <= ($NUM_TRANS_GROUPS - 1)) 
    $ii := %range[0]
    while($ii <= %range[1]) 
      $iii := 1
      while($iii <= 120) 
        wait_longer
        $blip_note := play_note($ii, $iii, 0, - 1)
        set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
        change_vol($blip_note, - 2000000, 0)
        set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $trans_group + $u)
        wait_longer
        $zone_id := get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
        if(($zone_id # -1) and ($zone_id # 0))
          if(search(%zone_ids_master, $zone_id) = -1)
            $trans_idx := search(%zone_ids_master, - 1)
            if(1 = $TRUE)
              %zone_ids_master[$trans_idx] := (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))
            else
              %zone_ids_master[$trans_idx] := $zone_id
            end if
            !file_names_master[$trans_idx] := get_sample($zone_id, $NI_FILE_NAME)
            %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$trans_idx] := $u
            set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($btn_filename), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !file_names_master[$trans_idx])
            set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scanningList), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
            set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_noInput), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
            set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scanningSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
          end if
        end if
        fade_out($blip_note, 0, 1)
        $iii := $iii + 5
      end while
      wait_longer
      inc($ii)
    end while
    wait_longer
    inc($u)
  end while
  $NUM_TRANS_SAMPLES := search(%zone_ids_master, - 1)
  $NUM_TRANS_SAMPLES_PLAYED := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
  save_array_str(%zone_ids_master, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "zone_ids_master.nka")
  save_array_str(!file_names_master, @legato_path & !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] & "file_names_master.nka")
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scanningList), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scanningSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_noInput), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_sModInd), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fadeInCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fadeOutCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_waitTime), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
end function
function update__eqBandwidth
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par($ENGINE_PAR_BW1, get_ui_id($sli_eqBandwidth), %vibrato_groups[$i], 5, 1)
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
function reset__label_texts
  set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_volume), "Zone Vol.")
  set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestart), "S. Start")
  set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_waitSus), "Wait Time")
  set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), "Release")
  set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_fadeInSus), "Fade In")
  set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_fadeInTrans), "Fade In")
  set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_fadeOutTrans), "Fade Out")
end function
function update__vibIntensity
  $sli_vibrato := $sli_vibIntensity
  call update__cc_vibrato
end function
function update__vibrato
  $sli_vibIntensity := $sli_vibrato
  call update__cc_vibrato
end function
function release_notes
  if((get_event_mark($release_id, $MARK_1) = $TRUE) and ($event_id = $release_id))
    message("release group triggered")
    $count := 0
    if($is_attack = $FALSE)
      message("no attack")
      $release_id := play_note(get_event_par($event_id, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE), $EVENT_VELOCITY, 0, 0)
      set_event_par_arr($release_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
      $i := 0
      while($i <= ($NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER - 1)) 
        set_event_par_arr($release_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $i + $sus_rls_group)
        inc($i)
      end while
    end if
    fade_out($event_id, 200000, 1)
    %event_notes[$release_note] := - 1
    $release_note := $event_note
    if(- sh_right(abs(%development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
      call reset__label_texts
    end if
  end if
end function
function update__gui__legato
  call update__infolabels
  $btn_markSample := %marked_samples[$trans_idx]
  call update__sampleComment
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_sModRange), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "S. Mod: " & get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_SAMPLE_MOD_RANGE))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_sModInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_SAMPLE_MOD_RANGE) - 0) * 99) / (get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_SAMPLE_END) - 0))
  $sli_volume := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%trans_event_volume[$trans_idx]) - -10000.0) * 1000000.0) / 20000.0) + 0.0)
  $sli_samplestart := real_to_int((((((int_to_real(%trans_zone_start[$trans_idx]) / 48000.0) * 1000000.0) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / (int_to_real($max_samplestart * 1000) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
  call update__zoneVolume
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, real_to_int((((int_to_real(%trans_zone_start[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_end) - 0.0)) + 0.0))
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestart), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, ((($sli_samplestart - 0) * ($max_samplestart - 0)) / 1000000) & " ms")
  $sli_fadeInTrans := %trans_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInTrans
  $sli_fadeOutTrans := %trans_fadeOut_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeOutTrans
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_completed), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, %completed_elements[$element__idx])
end function
function update__cc_dynamics
  set_controller(103, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_dynamics)) - 0.0) * 127.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0))
  $v := 0
  while($v <= (num_elements(get_ui_id(%lbl_sus_filename)) - 1)) 
    set_control_par(%lbl_sus_filename[$v], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[0])
    inc($v)
  end while
  set_control_par(%lbl_sus_filename[real_to_int((((int_to_real($sli_dynamics) - 0.0) * (int_to_real($NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER - 1) - 0.0)) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[2])
end function
function delete__preset
  %vibrato_preset[$preset_idx__DELETED] := $TRUE
  save_array_str(%vibrato_preset, @base_path & !vibPresetNames[$mnu_preset] & ".nka")
  $ii := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%vibPresetCount) - 1)) 
    if($i # $mnu_preset)
      !vibPresetNames[$ii] := !vibPresetNames[$i]
      %vibPresetCount[$ii] := %vibPresetCount[$i]
      inc($ii)
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  save__resource_arrays
  $presetCount := ((($presetCount - 1) * (1 + (sh_right(100 - ($presetCount - 1), 31) .or. sh_right(($presetCount - 1) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(($presetCount - 1) - 0, 31))) - (100 * sh_right(100 - ($presetCount - 1), 31))
  $mnu_preset := ((($mnu_preset - 1) * (1 + (sh_right($presetCount - ($mnu_preset - 1), 31) .or. sh_right(($mnu_preset - 1) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(($mnu_preset - 1) - 0, 31))) - ($presetCount * sh_right($presetCount - ($mnu_preset - 1), 31))
  call update__preset__menu
  if($presetCount # 0)
    load__preset
  end if
end function
function update__keycolor
  $keys := 0
  while($keys <= 127) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_INACTIVE)
    if(in_range($keys, %range[0], %range[1]))
      set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    end if
    inc($keys)
  end while
end function
function init__arrays
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 1999) 
    if(%sus_release_time[$i] = 0)
      %sus_release_time[$i] := $DEFAULT_VAL__sus_release_time
    end if
    if(%trans_fadeIn_time[$i] = 0)
      %trans_fadeIn_time[$i] := $DEFAULT_VAL__trans_fadeIn_time
    end if
    if(%trans_fadeOut_time[$i] = 0)
      %trans_fadeOut_time[$i] := $DEFAULT_VAL__trans_fadeOut_time
    end if
    if(%trans_wait_time[$i] = 0)
      %trans_wait_time[$i] := $DEFAULT_VAL__trans_wait_time
    end if
    if(%sus_fadeIn_time[$i] = 0)
      %sus_fadeIn_time[$i] := $DEFAULT_VAL__sus_fadeIn_time
    end if
    if(%trans_zone_ids[$i] = 0)
      %trans_zone_ids[$i] := - 1
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
end function
on persistence_changed
  if($pgs_init = 0)
    $pgs_init := 1
    call load__arrays
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_loadedData), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx])
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(@txt_loadedData), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx])
    if(- sh_right(abs(%development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
      $btn_home := $FALSE
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_home), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_reverb), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_eq), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
      $btn_settings := $FALSE
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_settings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
      $btn_legatoSettings := $FALSE
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_dataSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_waveform), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_sustainSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_resetWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])

      $num_notes := %KEY_DOWN[$i] + $num_notes
      inc($i)
    end while
    $interval := $EVENT_NOTE - $last_note
    if((($num_notes > 1) and ($EVENT_NOTE # $last_note)) and ($is_attack # -1))
      $is_attack := $FALSE
      if(abs($interval) <= 12)
        if(- sh_right(abs(%development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)

            set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
            inc($keys)

        end if

        change_vol($blip_note, - 200000, 0)

          $i := 0

            if(in_range($EVENT_VELOCITY, %_trans_ranges[$i * 2], %_trans_ranges[($i * 2) + 1]))
              $current_trans_group := $trans_group + $i
            end if
            inc($i)
          end while
        else
          if($mnu_rr = ($NUM_TRANS_GROUPS + 1))
            %_trans_rr[(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)] := (%_trans_rr[(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)] + 1) mod $NUM_TRANS_GROUPS
            $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %_trans_rr[(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)]
          else
            $current_trans_group := $trans_group + $mnu_rr
          end if
        end if
