            $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
          else
            $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
          end if
        else
          if(search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = -1)
            $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
          else
            $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
          end if
        end if
        if(1 = $TRUE)
          %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))
        else
          %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
        end if
        fade_out($event_id, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] * 1000, 1)
        fade_out($attack_id, 200000, 1)
        fade_out($last_transition, 200000, 1)
        fade_out($blip_note, 0, 1)
        $transition_id := play_note(($EVENT_NOTE * abs(sh_right(abs(sh_right($interval - 0, 31) + 1) - 1, 31))) + ($last_note * (sh_right($interval - 0, 31) + 1)), (abs($interval) * 5) + ((sh_right($interval - 0, 31) + 1) * 60), real_to_int((int_to_real(%trans_zone_start[$trans_idx]) / 48000.0) * 1000000.0), 0)
        if($mnu_rr = $NUM_TRANS_GROUPS)
          $i := 0
          while($i <= ($NUM_TRANS_GROUPS - 1)) 
            if(in_range($EVENT_VELOCITY, %_trans_ranges[$i * 2], %_trans_ranges[($i * 2) + 1]))
              $current_trans_group := $trans_group + $i
            end if
            inc($i)
          end while
        else
          if($mnu_rr = ($NUM_TRANS_GROUPS + 1))
            %_trans_rr[(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)] := (%_trans_rr[(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)] + 1) mod $NUM_TRANS_GROUPS
            $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %_trans_rr[(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)]
          else
            $current_trans_group := $trans_group + $mnu_rr
          end if
        end if
        set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
        set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, %trans_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx], 3)
        set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, %trans_fadeOut_time[$trans_idx], 5)
        $play_event := get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE)
        $play_velo := get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY)
        if($btn_legato = $TRUE)
          set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $current_trans_group)
          change_vol($transition_id, %trans_event_volume[$trans_idx], 0)
          if(- sh_right(abs(%development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
            wait(1)
            %trans_zone_volume[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
            %trans_zone_pan[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_PAN)
            !trans_file_names[$trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $NI_FILE_NAME)
            attach_zone(get_ui_id($wf_transition), get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
            %btn_elements_onoff[0 - ((0 - $element__idx) .and. sh_right(0 - $element__idx, 31))] := 0
            $element__idx := 0 - ((0 - search(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids, %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx])) .and. sh_right(0 - search(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids, %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx]), 31))
            %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 1
            if(get_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_legatoList), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE) = $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
              $loc_22 := 0
              $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD := $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS
              $NUM_PRESETS := search(%zone_ids_master, - 1)
              $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS := $NUM_PRESETS
              set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_presetcount), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS & "/" & $NUM_PRESETS)
              if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD # $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
                $loc_22 := 0
                while($loc_22 <= (num_elements(%legatoList__end_of_list) - 1)) 
                  %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_22] := - 1
                  if($loc_22 < $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
                    %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_22] := 1
                  end if
                  inc($loc_22)
                end while
              end if
              $scroll__up := real_to_int((((~scroll__realup - 0.0) * (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD - 12) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
              call update__preset_button_focus
              call update__scrollbar
              call update__scrollarea
              if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS > 12)
                $sli_scrollbar := 1000000 - ((1000000 / ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12)) * $scroll__up)
                set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_MOUSE_BEHAVIOUR, - (4248 + (2 * ($NUM_PRESETS - $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS))))
                $handle_size := real_to_int(round(int_to_real(245) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS) / int_to_real(12))))
                if($handle_size < 30)
                  $handle_size := 30
                end if
              else
                $sli_scrollbar := 1000000
                $handle_size := 245
              end if
              set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, $handle_size)
              set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + ((245 - $handle_size) - (($sli_scrollbar * (245 - $handle_size)) / 1000000)))
            end if
            call update__gui__legato
            !intervals[$trans_idx] := @playedInterval
          end if
        end if
        if($btn_sus = $TRUE)
          $event_id := play_note($EVENT_NOTE, $EVENT_VELOCITY, $sus_s_start, - 1)
          set_event_mark($event_id, $MARK_1)
          %sus_rr[$EVENT_NOTE] := (%sus_rr[$EVENT_NOTE] + 1) mod 3
          set_event_par_arr($event_id, $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx], 0)
          set_event_par_arr($event_id, $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx], 2)
          if(- sh_right(abs(%development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
            $sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%sus_release_time[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000.0) + 0.0)
            ~loc_21 := 0.0
            %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
            set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
            ~loc_21 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
            set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_21 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_21 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_21 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_21 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_21 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
            set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
            $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
            call update__waitSus
            $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
            call update__fadeInSus
          end if
        end if
        set_event_par_arr($event_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
        $i := 0
        while($i <= ($NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER - 1)) 
          set_event_par_arr($event_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $i + $sus_group)
          inc($i)
        end while
        $i := 0
        while($i <= $NUM_SUSTAIN_FX_GROUPS) 
          set_event_par_arr($event_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $i + $sus_fx_group)
          inc($i)
        end while
      else
        fade_out($event_id, 152000, 1)
        $event_id := play_note($EVENT_NOTE, $EVENT_VELOCITY, $sus_s_start, - 1)
        set_event_par_arr($event_id, $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, 150000, 0)
        set_event_par_arr($event_id, $EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, $DEFAULT_VAL__sus_fadeIn_time, 2)
        set_event_par_arr($event_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
        $i := 0
        while($i <= ($NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER - 1)) 
          set_event_par_arr($event_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $i + $sus_group)
          inc($i)
        end while
        $i := 0
        while($i <= $NUM_SUSTAIN_FX_GROUPS) 
          set_event_par_arr($event_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $i + $sus_fx_group)
          inc($i)
        end while
      end if
    else
      if($num_notes = 1)
        $last_note := $event_note
        if((1 + sh_right(abs($NUM_ATK_GROUPS) - 1, 31)) = $TRUE)
          $is_attack := - 1
          wait(90000)
          $is_attack := abs(sh_right(abs($NOTE_HELD) - 1, 31))
        else
          $is_attack := $FALSE
        end if
        set_event_par_arr($ALL_EVENTS, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
        $event_id := play_note($EVENT_NOTE, $EVENT_VELOCITY, $sus_s_start, - 1)
        set_event_mark($event_id, $MARK_1)
        $attack_id := play_note($EVENT_NOTE, %CC[103], 0, 0)
        if($btn_sus = $TRUE)
          set_event_par_arr($event_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
          $iii := 0
          while($iii <= ($NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER - 1)) 
            set_event_par_arr($event_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $iii + $atk_sus_group)
            inc($iii)
          end while
          $iii := 0
          while($iii <= $NUM_SUSTAIN_FX_GROUPS) 
            set_event_par_arr($event_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $iii + $sus_fx_group)
            inc($iii)
          end while
          if((1 + sh_right(abs($NUM_ATK_GROUPS) - 1, 31)) = $TRUE)
            set_event_par_arr($attack_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $atk_group + %rr_count[$EVENT_NOTE])
            %rr_count[$EVENT_NOTE] := (%rr_count[$EVENT_NOTE] + 1) mod $NUM_ATK_GROUPS
          end if
        end if
      else
        note_off($event_id)
      end if
    end if
    $last_transition := $transition_id
    $last_note := $event_note
    $release_note := - 1
  end if
  %event_notes[$event_note] := $event_note
end on
on release
  $release_note := $EVENT_NOTE
  $release_id := $EVENT_ID
  call release_notes
  set_key_pressed($EVENT_NOTE, 0)
end on
on ui_control($mnu_rr)
  if($mnu_rr = $NUM_TRANS_GROUPS)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= ($NUM_TRANS_GROUPS - 1)) 
      if(in_range($play_velo, %_trans_ranges[$i * 2], %_trans_ranges[($i * 2) + 1]))
        $current_trans_group := $trans_group + $i
      end if
      inc($i)
    end while
  else
    if($mnu_rr = ($NUM_TRANS_GROUPS + 1))
      %_trans_rr[(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)] := (%_trans_rr[(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)] + 1) mod $NUM_TRANS_GROUPS
      $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %_trans_rr[(get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)]
    else
      $current_trans_group := $trans_group + $mnu_rr
    end if
  end if
  $transition_id := play_note($play_event, $play_velo, 0, - 1)
  change_vol($transition_id, - 200000, 0)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
  if($mnu_rr = $NUM_TRANS_GROUPS)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= ($NUM_TRANS_GROUPS - 1)) 
      if(in_range($play_velo, %_trans_ranges[$i * 2], %_trans_ranges[($i * 2) + 1]))
        $current_trans_group := $trans_group + $i
      end if
      inc($i)
    end while
  else
    if($mnu_rr = ($NUM_TRANS_GROUPS + 1))
      %_trans_rr[(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)] := (%_trans_rr[(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)] + 1) mod $NUM_TRANS_GROUPS
      $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %_trans_rr[(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)]
    else
      $current_trans_group := $trans_group + $mnu_rr
    end if
  end if
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $current_trans_group)
  wait(1)
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
    end if
  else
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
    end if
  end if
  attach_zone(get_ui_id($wf_transition), get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
  %btn_elements_onoff[0 - ((0 - $element__idx) .and. sh_right(0 - $element__idx, 31))] := 0
  $element__idx := 0 - ((0 - search(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids, %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx])) .and. sh_right(0 - search(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids, %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx]), 31))
  %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 1
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))
  else
    %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
  end if
  %trans_zone_volume[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
  %trans_zone_pan[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_PAN)
  !trans_file_names[$trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $NI_FILE_NAME)
  fade_out($transition_id, 0, 1)
  call update__gui__legato
  $sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%sus_release_time[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000.0) + 0.0)
  ~loc_23 := 0.0
  %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_23 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
end on
on ui_control($btn_play)
  call play_trans_sample
end on
on ui_control($btn_reset)
  $btn_reset := $FALSE
  call reset__label_texts
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%check_button_state) - 1)) 
    set_control_par(%check_button_state[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, $TRUE)
    inc($i)
  end while
  $btn_check_markSample := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_forallWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($TRUE) - 1, 31))])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_resetWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$TRUE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$TRUE])
end on
on ui_control($btn_cancel)
  $btn_cancel := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_resetWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
end on
on ui_control($btn_ok)
  $btn_ok := $FALSE
  $loc_11 := 0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(%check_button_state) - 1)) 
    $loc_11 := $loc_11 + get_control_par(%check_button_state[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 1999) 
    if($loc_11 = num_elements(%check_button_state))
      !trans_file_names[$i] := ""
      %trans_zone_ids[$i] := - 1
      !file_names_master[$i] := ""
      %zone_ids_master[$i] := - 1
      !samples_to_revisit[$i] := ""
      !intervals[$i] := ""
      !sus_file_names[$i] := ""
      %sus_zone_ids[$i] := - 1
      %sus_zone_volume[$i] := 0
    end if
    %sus_release_time[$i] := %sus_release_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_releaseSus) - 1, 31))
    %trans_zone_start[$i] := %trans_zone_start[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_samplestart) - 1, 31))
    %trans_event_volume[$i] := %trans_event_volume[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_volume) - 1, 31))
    %trans_wait_time[$i] := %trans_wait_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_waitSus) - 1, 31))
    %sus_fadeIn_time[$i] := %sus_fadeIn_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeInSus) - 1, 31))
    %trans_fadeIn_time[$i] := %trans_fadeIn_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeInTrans) - 1, 31))
    %trans_fadeOut_time[$i] := %trans_fadeOut_time[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_fadeOutTrans) - 1, 31))
    %marked_samples[$i] := %marked_samples[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_markSample) - 1, 31))
    if($btn_check_markSample = $TRUE)
      !sample_comments[$i] := ""
    end if
    %completed_elements[$i] := %completed_elements[$i] * abs(sh_right(abs($btn_check_completed) - 1, 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  call save__arrays
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_resetWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  call init__arrays
  $transition_id := play_note($play_event, $play_velo, 0, - 1)
  change_vol($transition_id, - 200000, 0)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
  if($mnu_rr = $NUM_TRANS_GROUPS)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= ($NUM_TRANS_GROUPS - 1)) 
      if(in_range($play_velo, %_trans_ranges[$i * 2], %_trans_ranges[($i * 2) + 1]))
        $current_trans_group := $trans_group + $i
      end if
      inc($i)
    end while
  else
    if($mnu_rr = ($NUM_TRANS_GROUPS + 1))
      %_trans_rr[(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)] := (%_trans_rr[(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)] + 1) mod $NUM_TRANS_GROUPS
      $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %_trans_rr[(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)]
    else
      $current_trans_group := $trans_group + $mnu_rr
    end if
  end if
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $current_trans_group)
  wait(1)
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
    end if
  else
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
    end if
  end if
  attach_zone(get_ui_id($wf_transition), get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
  %btn_elements_onoff[0 - ((0 - $element__idx) .and. sh_right(0 - $element__idx, 31))] := 0
  $element__idx := 0 - ((0 - search(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids, %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx])) .and. sh_right(0 - search(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids, %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx]), 31))

    %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))
  else
    %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
  end if

  %trans_zone_pan[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_PAN)
  !trans_file_names[$trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $NI_FILE_NAME)
  fade_out($transition_id, 0, 1)
  call update__gui__legato
  $sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%sus_release_time[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000.0) + 0.0)
  ~loc_23 := 0.0
  %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_23 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0

  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))

    end while
    $loc_13 := 0
    while($loc_13 <= ($NUM_TRANS_SAMPLES_PLAYED - 1)) 
      $loc_12 := search(%zone_ids_master, %trans_zone_ids[$loc_13])
      if($loc_12 # -1)
        %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_12] := %marked_samples[$loc_13]
        !legatoList__intervals[$loc_12] := !intervals[$loc_13]
        !legatoList__comments[$loc_12] := !sample_comments[$loc_13]
      end if
      inc($loc_13)
    end while
    $loc_11 := 0
    $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD := $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS
    $NUM_PRESETS := search(%zone_ids_master, - 1)
    $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS := $NUM_PRESETS
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_presetcount), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS & "/" & $NUM_PRESETS)
    if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD # $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
      $loc_11 := 0
      while($loc_11 <= (num_elements(%legatoList__end_of_list) - 1)) 
        %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := - 1
        if($loc_11 < $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
          %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := 1
        end if
        inc($loc_11)
      end while
    end if
    $scroll__up := real_to_int((((~scroll__realup - 0.0) * (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD - 12) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
    call update__preset_button_focus
    call update__scrollbar
    call update__scrollarea
    if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS > 12)
      $sli_scrollbar := 1000000 - ((1000000 / ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12)) * $scroll__up)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_MOUSE_BEHAVIOUR, - (4248 + (2 * ($NUM_PRESETS - $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS))))
      $handle_size := real_to_int(round(int_to_real(245) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS) / int_to_real(12))))
      if($handle_size < 30)
        $handle_size := 30
      end if
    else
      $sli_scrollbar := 1000000
      $handle_size := 245
    end if
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, $handle_size)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + ((245 - $handle_size) - (($sli_scrollbar * (245 - $handle_size)) / 1000000)))
  end if
  $btn_vibratoSettings := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  $btn_legatoSettings := $TRUE
  $btn_legatoSettings := $btn_legatoSettings
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_dataSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_waveform), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_sustainSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_resetWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_forallWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  call reset__label_texts
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
end on
on ui_control(@txt_loadedData)
  !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx] := get_control_par_str(get_ui_id(@txt_loadedData), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_loadedData), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx])
end on

  $NUM_ATK_GROUPS := $vlue_atkGroups
end on

on ui_control($btn_analyze)
  $atk_sus_group := ($title_groups + $NUM_ATK_GROUPS) + $title_groups
  message("atk_sus_group: " & $atk_sus_group)
  $keys := 0
  while($keys <= 127) 
    $blip_note := play_note($keys, 1, 0, 1)
    set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
    change_vol($blip_note, - 2000000, 0)
    set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $atk_sus_group)
    wait(1)
    $zone_id := get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
    if(($zone_id # -1) and ($zone_id # 0))
      %range[0] := $keys
      $keys := 127
    end if
    fade_out($blip_note, 0, 1)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  $keys := 0
  while($keys <= 127) 
    $blip_note := play_note(127 - $keys, 1, 0, - 1)
    set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
    change_vol($blip_note, - 2000000, 0)
    set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $atk_sus_group)
    wait(1)
    $zone_id := get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
    if(($zone_id # -1) and ($zone_id # 0))
      %range[1] := 127 - $keys
      $keys := 127
    end if
    fade_out($blip_note, 0, 1)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  call update__keycolor
  call load__arrays
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_loadedData), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx])
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(@txt_loadedData), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, !legato_prefixes[$prefix_idx])
  $iii := 0
  while($iii <= ($NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER - 1)) 
    $blip_note := play_note($event_note, 1, 1, - 1)
    change_vol($blip_note, - 200000, 0)
    set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
    set_event_par_arr($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $atk_sus_group + $iii)
    wait(1)
    %sus_zone_ids[$iii] := get_event_par($blip_note, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
    fade_out($blip_note, 0, 1)
    set_control_par_str(%lbl_sus_filename[$iii], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_sample(%sus_zone_ids[$iii], $NI_FILE_NAME))
    inc($iii)
  end while
  call scan__samples
  $transition_id := play_note($play_event, $play_velo, 0, - 1)
  change_vol($transition_id, - 200000, 0)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
  if($mnu_rr = $NUM_TRANS_GROUPS)
    $i := 0
    while($i <= ($NUM_TRANS_GROUPS - 1)) 
      if(in_range($play_velo, %_trans_ranges[$i * 2], %_trans_ranges[($i * 2) + 1]))
        $current_trans_group := $trans_group + $i
      end if
      inc($i)
    end while
  else
    if($mnu_rr = ($NUM_TRANS_GROUPS + 1))
      %_trans_rr[(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)] := (%_trans_rr[(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)] + 1) mod $NUM_TRANS_GROUPS
      $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %_trans_rr[(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)]
    else
      $current_trans_group := $trans_group + $mnu_rr
    end if
  end if
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $current_trans_group)
  wait(1)
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
    end if
  else
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
    end if
  end if
  attach_zone(get_ui_id($wf_transition), get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
  %btn_elements_onoff[0 - ((0 - $element__idx) .and. sh_right(0 - $element__idx, 31))] := 0
  $element__idx := 0 - ((0 - search(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids, %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx])) .and. sh_right(0 - search(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids, %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx]), 31))
  %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 1
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))
  else
    %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
  end if
  %trans_zone_volume[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
  %trans_zone_pan[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_PAN)
  !trans_file_names[$trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $NI_FILE_NAME)
  fade_out($transition_id, 0, 1)
  call update__gui__legato
  $sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%sus_release_time[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000.0) + 0.0)
  ~loc_24 := 0.0
  %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_24 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_24 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_24 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_24 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_24 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_24 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
  $loc_25 := 0
  $loc_26 := 0
  $loc_25 := 0
  while($loc_25 <= 1999) 
    %legatoList__element_numbers[$loc_25] := $loc_25
    !legatoList__trans_file_names[$loc_25] := !file_names_master[$loc_25]
    %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$loc_25] := %zone_ids_master[$loc_25]
    %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_25] := 0
    !legatoList__intervals[$loc_25] := ""
    !legatoList__comments[$loc_25] := ""
    inc($loc_25)
  end while
  $loc_25 := 0
  while($loc_25 <= ($NUM_TRANS_SAMPLES_PLAYED - 1)) 
    $loc_26 := search(%zone_ids_master, %trans_zone_ids[$loc_25])
    if($loc_26 # -1)
      %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_26] := %marked_samples[$loc_25]
      !legatoList__intervals[$loc_26] := !intervals[$loc_25]
      !legatoList__comments[$loc_26] := !sample_comments[$loc_25]
    end if
    inc($loc_25)
  end while
  $loc_27 := 0
  $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD := $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS
  $NUM_PRESETS := search(%zone_ids_master, - 1)
  $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS := $NUM_PRESETS
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_presetcount), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS & "/" & $NUM_PRESETS)
  if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD # $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
    $loc_27 := 0
    while($loc_27 <= (num_elements(%legatoList__end_of_list) - 1)) 
      %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_27] := - 1
      if($loc_27 < $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
        %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_27] := 1
      end if
      inc($loc_27)
    end while
  end if
  $scroll__up := real_to_int((((~scroll__realup - 0.0) * (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD - 12) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
  call update__preset_button_focus
  call update__scrollbar
  call update__scrollarea
  if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS > 12)
    $sli_scrollbar := 1000000 - ((1000000 / ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12)) * $scroll__up)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_MOUSE_BEHAVIOUR, - (4248 + (2 * ($NUM_PRESETS - $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS))))
    $handle_size := real_to_int(round(int_to_real(245) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS) / int_to_real(12))))
    if($handle_size < 30)
      $handle_size := 30
    end if
  else
    $sli_scrollbar := 1000000
    $handle_size := 245
  end if
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, $handle_size)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + ((245 - $handle_size) - (($sli_scrollbar * (245 - $handle_size)) / 1000000)))
  $btn_analyze := $FALSE
end on

on ui_control($sli_samplestart)
  $loc_28 := 0
  $slider := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_samplestart)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real($max_samplestart * 1000) - 0.0)) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  %trans_zone_start[$trans_idx] := ((real_to_int((int_to_real($slider) / 1000000.0) * 48000.0) * (1 + (sh_right($sample_end - real_to_int((int_to_real($slider) / 1000000.0) * 48000.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int((int_to_real($slider) / 1000000.0) * 48000.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int((int_to_real($slider) / 1000000.0) * 48000.0) - 0, 31))) - ($sample_end * sh_right($sample_end - real_to_int((int_to_real($slider) / 1000000.0) * 48000.0), 31))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, real_to_int((((int_to_real(%trans_zone_start[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_end) - 0.0)) + 0.0))
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestart), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, ((($sli_samplestart - 0) * ($max_samplestart - 0)) / 1000000) & " ms")
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fadeInCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_fadeOutCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  ~current_fadeInTime := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_fadeInSus)) - 0.0) * 500.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_waitTime), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~current_fadeInTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~current_fadeInTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~current_fadeInTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~current_fadeInTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~current_fadeInTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  ~current_waitTime := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_waitSus)) - 0.0) * 500.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_waitTime), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + 2) + real_to_int(((((~current_waitTime * 1000.0) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_waitTime), $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, (555 - get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_waitTime), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X)) - 2)
  $last_time_samplestart := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_samplestart) > 795)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestart), $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, 1)
    set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestart), "S. Start")
    call save__arrays
  end if
end on

  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_waitSus) > 795)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_waitSus), $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, 1)
    set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_waitSus), "Wait Time")
    call save__arrays
  end if
end on

on ui_control($sli_releaseSus)
  ~loc_29 := 0.0
  %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_29 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_29 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_29 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_29 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_29 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_29 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $last_time_releaseSus := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_releaseSus) > 795)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, 1)
    set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), "Release")
    call save__arrays
  end if
end on

  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_waveform), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])

  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_resetWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_forallWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])

  call reset__label_texts
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  $btn_legatoList := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_legatoList), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoList])
  if(- sh_right(abs(%development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
    $loc_13 := 0
    $loc_12 := 0
    $loc_13 := 0
    while($loc_13 <= 1999) 
      %legatoList__element_numbers[$loc_13] := $loc_13
      !legatoList__trans_file_names[$loc_13] := !file_names_master[$loc_13]
      %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$loc_13] := %zone_ids_master[$loc_13]
      %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_13] := 0
      !legatoList__intervals[$loc_13] := ""
      !legatoList__comments[$loc_13] := ""
      inc($loc_13)
    end while
    $loc_13 := 0
    while($loc_13 <= ($NUM_TRANS_SAMPLES_PLAYED - 1)) 
      $loc_12 := search(%zone_ids_master, %trans_zone_ids[$loc_13])
      if($loc_12 # -1)
        %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_12] := %marked_samples[$loc_13]
        !legatoList__intervals[$loc_12] := !intervals[$loc_13]
        !legatoList__comments[$loc_12] := !sample_comments[$loc_13]
      end if
      inc($loc_13)
    end while
    $loc_11 := 0
    $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD := $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS
    $NUM_PRESETS := search(%zone_ids_master, - 1)
    $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS := $NUM_PRESETS
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_presetcount), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS & "/" & $NUM_PRESETS)
    if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD # $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
      $loc_11 := 0
      while($loc_11 <= (num_elements(%legatoList__end_of_list) - 1)) 
        %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := - 1
        if($loc_11 < $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
          %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := 1
        end if
        inc($loc_11)
      end while
    end if
    $scroll__up := real_to_int((((~scroll__realup - 0.0) * (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD - 12) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
    call update__preset_button_focus
    call update__scrollbar
    call update__scrollarea
    if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS > 12)
      $sli_scrollbar := 1000000 - ((1000000 / ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12)) * $scroll__up)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_MOUSE_BEHAVIOUR, - (4248 + (2 * ($NUM_PRESETS - $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS))))
      $handle_size := real_to_int(round(int_to_real(245) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS) / int_to_real(12))))
      if($handle_size < 30)
        $handle_size := 30
      end if
    else
      $sli_scrollbar := 1000000
      $handle_size := 245
    end if
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, $handle_size)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + ((245 - $handle_size) - (($sli_scrollbar * (245 - $handle_size)) / 1000000)))
  end if
  $btn_vibratoSettings := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  $btn_legatoList := $TRUE
  $btn_legatoList := $btn_legatoList
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_legatoList), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoList])

      while($loc_11 <= (num_elements(%legatoList__end_of_list) - 1)) 
        %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := - 1
        if($loc_11 < $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
          %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := 1
        end if
        inc($loc_11)
      end while
    end if
    $scroll__up := real_to_int((((~scroll__realup - 0.0) * (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD - 12) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
    call update__preset_button_focus
    call update__scrollbar
    call update__scrollarea
    if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS > 12)
      $sli_scrollbar := 1000000 - ((1000000 / ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12)) * $scroll__up)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_MOUSE_BEHAVIOUR, - (4248 + (2 * ($NUM_PRESETS - $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS))))
      $handle_size := real_to_int(round(int_to_real(245) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS) / int_to_real(12))))
      if($handle_size < 30)
        $handle_size := 30
      end if
    else
      $sli_scrollbar := 1000000
      $handle_size := 245
    end if
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, $handle_size)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + ((245 - $handle_size) - (($sli_scrollbar * (245 - $handle_size)) / 1000000)))
  end if
  $btn_vibratoSettings := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  $btn_legatoSettings := $TRUE
  $btn_legatoSettings := $btn_legatoSettings
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_dataSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_waveform), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_sustainSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_resetWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_forallWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  call reset__label_texts
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
end on

on ui_control($btn_prev)
  $btn_prev := $FALSE
  %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 0
  set_control_par(%btn_element_button[$element__idx - $scroll__up], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
  set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + ($element__idx - $scroll__up)], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[0])
  set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + ($element__idx - $scroll__up)], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[0])
  set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + ($element__idx - $scroll__up)], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[0])
  if($element__idx # -1)
    $element__idx := %legatoList__element_numbers[(($element__idx - 1) + $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS) mod $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS]
  else
    $element__idx := %legatoList__element_numbers[$element__idx - 1]
  end if
  %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 1
  if(($element__idx - $scroll__up) = -1)
    set_control_par(%btn_element_button[($element__idx - $scroll__up) + 1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + (($element__idx - $scroll__up) + 1)], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[2])
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + (($element__idx - $scroll__up) + 1)], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[2])
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + (($element__idx - $scroll__up) + 1)], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[2])
  else
    set_control_par(%btn_element_button[($element__idx - $scroll__up) - ((($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 11) .and. sh_right(11 - ($element__idx - $scroll__up), 31))], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + (($element__idx - $scroll__up) - ((($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 11) .and. sh_right(11 - ($element__idx - $scroll__up), 31)))], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[2])
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + (($element__idx - $scroll__up) - ((($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 11) .and. sh_right(11 - ($element__idx - $scroll__up), 31)))], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[2])
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + (($element__idx - $scroll__up) - ((($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 11) .and. sh_right(11 - ($element__idx - $scroll__up), 31)))], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[2])
  end if
  if(not in_range($element__idx, $scroll__up, ($scroll__up + 12) - 1))
    dec($scroll__up)
    call update__preset_button_focus
    call update__scrollbar
    call update__scrollarea
  end if
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    $play_event := lsb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
    $play_velo := msb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
  else
    $play_event := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)
    $play_velo := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_LOW_VELO)
  end if
  $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $mnu_rr := %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $transition_id := play_note($play_event, $play_velo, 0, - 1)
  change_vol($transition_id, - 200000, 0)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $current_trans_group)
  wait(1)
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
    end if
  else
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
    end if
  end if
  attach_zone(get_ui_id($wf_transition), get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx]
  %trans_zone_volume[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
  %trans_zone_pan[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_PAN)
  !trans_file_names[$trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $NI_FILE_NAME)
  note_off($transition_id)
  call update__gui__legato
  $sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%sus_release_time[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000.0) + 0.0)
  ~loc_30 := 0.0
  %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_30 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_30 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_30 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_30 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_30 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_30 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
  $keys := %range[0]
  while($keys <= %range[1]) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  if($btn_mute = $TRUE)
    call play_trans_sample
  end if
end on
on ui_control($btn_next)
  $btn_next := $FALSE
  %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 0
  set_control_par(%btn_element_button[$element__idx - $scroll__up], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
  set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + ($element__idx - $scroll__up)], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[0])
  set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + ($element__idx - $scroll__up)], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[0])
  set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + ($element__idx - $scroll__up)], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[0])
  if($element__idx # -1)
    $element__idx := %legatoList__element_numbers[($element__idx + 1) mod $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS]
  else
    $element__idx := %legatoList__element_numbers[0]
  end if
  %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 1
  if(($element__idx - $scroll__up) >= 12)
    set_control_par(%btn_element_button[($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 1], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + (($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 1)], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[2])
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + (($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 1)], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[2])
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + (($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 1)], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[2])
  else
    set_control_par(%btn_element_button[($element__idx - $scroll__up) - ((($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 0) .and. sh_right(($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 0, 31))], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + (($element__idx - $scroll__up) - ((($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 0) .and. sh_right(($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 0, 31)))], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[2])
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + (($element__idx - $scroll__up) - ((($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 0) .and. sh_right(($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 0, 31)))], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[2])
    set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + (($element__idx - $scroll__up) - ((($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 0) .and. sh_right(($element__idx - $scroll__up) - 0, 31)))], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[2])
  end if
  if(not in_range($element__idx, $scroll__up, ($scroll__up + 12) - 1))
    inc($scroll__up)
    if($scroll__up > $element__idx)
      $scroll__up := $element__idx
    else
      if(($element__idx - $scroll__up) > 12)
        $scroll__up := ($element__idx - 12) + 2
      end if
    end if
    call update__scrollbar
    call update__scrollarea
  end if
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    $play_event := lsb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
    $play_velo := msb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
  else
    $play_event := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)
    $play_velo := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_LOW_VELO)
  end if
  $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $mnu_rr := %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $transition_id := play_note($play_event, $play_velo, 0, - 1)
  change_vol($transition_id, - 200000, 0)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $current_trans_group)
  wait(1)
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
    end if
  else
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
    end if
  end if
  attach_zone(get_ui_id($wf_transition), get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx]
  %trans_zone_volume[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
  %trans_zone_pan[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_PAN)
  !trans_file_names[$trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $NI_FILE_NAME)
  note_off($transition_id)
  call update__gui__legato
  $sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%sus_release_time[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000.0) + 0.0)
  ~loc_23 := 0.0
  %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_23 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
  $keys := %range[0]
  while($keys <= %range[1]) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  if($btn_mute = $TRUE)
    call play_trans_sample
  end if
end on
on ui_control($sli_scrollbar)
  if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS > 12)
    $scroll__up := ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - ((($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) * $sli_scrollbar) / 1000000)
    $scroll__up := $scroll__up
    ~scroll__realup := int_to_real($scroll__up)
    call update__scrollarea
  end if
end on

  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_23 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
  $keys := %range[0]
  while($keys <= %range[1]) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  call play_trans_sample
  call save__arrays
end on
on ui_control(@txt_element_marked1)
  !legatoList__comments[1 + $scroll__up] := get_control_par_str(@txt_element_marked1, $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT)
  if(search(%trans_zone_ids, %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[1 + $scroll__up]) = -1)
    $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
  else
    $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[1 + $scroll__up])
  end if
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[1 + $scroll__up]
  !sample_comments[$trans_idx] := get_control_par_str(@txt_element_marked1, $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT)
  call save__arrays
  call update__gui__legato
end on
on ui_control($btn_element_completed2)
  %completed_elements[%legatoList__element_numbers[2 + $scroll__up]] := get_control_par($btn_element_completed2, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)

  call update__gui__legato

on ui_control($btn_element_marked2)
  %legatoList__marked_elements[%legatoList__element_numbers[2 + $scroll__up]] := get_control_par($btn_element_marked2, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
  set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[2], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[get_control_par($btn_element_marked2, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)])
  set_control_par_str(!txt_element_marked[2], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "Comment and hit [Enter]")
  if(search(%trans_zone_ids, %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[2 + $scroll__up]) = -1)
    $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
  else
    $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[2 + $scroll__up])
  end if
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[2 + $scroll__up]
  %marked_samples[$trans_idx] := get_control_par($btn_element_marked2, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
  call save__arrays
  call update__gui__legato
end on
on ui_control($btn_element_played2)
  $btn_element_played2 := $FALSE
  %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 0
  $element__idx := 2 + $scroll__up
  %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 1
  call update__scrollbar
  call update__scrollarea
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    $play_event := lsb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
    $play_velo := msb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
  else
    $play_event := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)
    $play_velo := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_LOW_VELO)
  end if
  $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $mnu_rr := %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $transition_id := play_note($play_event, $play_velo, 0, - 1)
  change_vol($transition_id, - 200000, 0)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $current_trans_group)
  wait(1)
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
    end if
  else
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
    end if
  end if
  attach_zone(get_ui_id($wf_transition), get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx]
  %trans_zone_volume[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
  %trans_zone_pan[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_PAN)
  !trans_file_names[$trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $NI_FILE_NAME)
  note_off($transition_id)
  call update__gui__legato
  $sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%sus_release_time[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000.0) + 0.0)
  ~loc_23 := 0.0
  %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_23 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
  $keys := %range[0]
  while($keys <= %range[1]) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  call play_trans_sample
  call save__arrays
end on

  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
  $keys := %range[0]
  while($keys <= %range[1]) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  call play_trans_sample
  call save__arrays
end on
on ui_control(@txt_element_marked4)
  !legatoList__comments[4 + $scroll__up] := get_control_par_str(@txt_element_marked4, $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT)
  if(search(%trans_zone_ids, %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[4 + $scroll__up]) = -1)
    $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
  else
    $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[4 + $scroll__up])
  end if
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[4 + $scroll__up]
  !sample_comments[$trans_idx] := get_control_par_str(@txt_element_marked4, $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT)
  call save__arrays
  call update__gui__legato
end on
on ui_control($btn_element_completed5)
  %completed_elements[%legatoList__element_numbers[5 + $scroll__up]] := get_control_par($btn_element_completed5, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
  call save__completed_array
  call update__gui__legato
end on
on ui_control($btn_element_marked5)
  %legatoList__marked_elements[%legatoList__element_numbers[5 + $scroll__up]] := get_control_par($btn_element_marked5, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
  set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[5], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[get_control_par($btn_element_marked5, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)])
  set_control_par_str(!txt_element_marked[5], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "Comment and hit [Enter]")
  if(search(%trans_zone_ids, %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[5 + $scroll__up]) = -1)
    $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
  else
    $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[5 + $scroll__up])
  end if
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[5 + $scroll__up]
  %marked_samples[$trans_idx] := get_control_par($btn_element_marked5, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
  call save__arrays
  call update__gui__legato
end on
on ui_control($btn_element_played5)
  $btn_element_played5 := $FALSE
  %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 0
  $element__idx := 5 + $scroll__up
  %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 1
  call update__scrollbar
  call update__scrollarea
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    $play_event := lsb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
    $play_velo := msb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
  else
    $play_event := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)
    $play_velo := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_LOW_VELO)
  end if
  $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $mnu_rr := %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $transition_id := play_note($play_event, $play_velo, 0, - 1)
  change_vol($transition_id, - 200000, 0)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $current_trans_group)
  wait(1)
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
    end if
  else
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
    end if
  end if
  attach_zone(get_ui_id($wf_transition), get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx]
  %trans_zone_volume[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
  %trans_zone_pan[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_PAN)
  !trans_file_names[$trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $NI_FILE_NAME)
  note_off($transition_id)
  call update__gui__legato
  $sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%sus_release_time[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000.0) + 0.0)
  ~loc_23 := 0.0
  %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_23 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
  $keys := %range[0]
  while($keys <= %range[1]) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  call play_trans_sample
  call save__arrays
end on

  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
  $keys := %range[0]
  while($keys <= %range[1]) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  call play_trans_sample
  call save__arrays
end on
on ui_control(@txt_element_marked7)
  !legatoList__comments[7 + $scroll__up] := get_control_par_str(@txt_element_marked7, $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT)
  if(search(%trans_zone_ids, %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[7 + $scroll__up]) = -1)
    $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
  else
    $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[7 + $scroll__up])
  end if
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[7 + $scroll__up]
  !sample_comments[$trans_idx] := get_control_par_str(@txt_element_marked7, $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT)
  call save__arrays
  call update__gui__legato

on ui_control($btn_element_completed8)
