on ui_control($btn_element_marked8)
  %legatoList__marked_elements[%legatoList__element_numbers[8 + $scroll__up]] := get_control_par($btn_element_marked8, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
  set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[8], $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[get_control_par($btn_element_marked8, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)])
  set_control_par_str(!txt_element_marked[8], $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "Comment and hit [Enter]")
  if(search(%trans_zone_ids, %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[8 + $scroll__up]) = -1)
    $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
  else
    $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[8 + $scroll__up])
  end if
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[8 + $scroll__up]
  %marked_samples[$trans_idx] := get_control_par($btn_element_marked8, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
  call save__arrays
  call update__gui__legato
end on
on ui_control($btn_element_played8)
  $btn_element_played8 := $FALSE
  %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 0
  $element__idx := 8 + $scroll__up
  %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 1
  call update__scrollbar
  call update__scrollarea
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    $play_event := lsb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
    $play_velo := msb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
  else
    $play_event := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)
    $play_velo := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_LOW_VELO)
  end if
  $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $mnu_rr := %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $transition_id := play_note($play_event, $play_velo, 0, - 1)
  change_vol($transition_id, - 200000, 0)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $current_trans_group)
  wait(1)
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
    end if
  else
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
    end if
  end if
  attach_zone(get_ui_id($wf_transition), get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx]
  %trans_zone_volume[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
  %trans_zone_pan[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_PAN)
  !trans_file_names[$trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $NI_FILE_NAME)
  note_off($transition_id)
  call update__gui__legato
  $sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%sus_release_time[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000.0) + 0.0)
  ~loc_23 := 0.0
  %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_23 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
  $keys := %range[0]
  while($keys <= %range[1]) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  call play_trans_sample
  call save__arrays
end on

  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
  $keys := %range[0]
  while($keys <= %range[1]) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  call play_trans_sample
  call save__arrays
end on

on ui_control($btn_element_played11)
  $btn_element_played11 := $FALSE
  %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 0
  $element__idx := 11 + $scroll__up
  %btn_elements_onoff[$element__idx] := 1
  call update__scrollbar
  call update__scrollarea
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    $play_event := lsb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
    $play_velo := msb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
  else
    $play_event := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)
    $play_velo := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_LOW_VELO)
  end if
  $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $mnu_rr := %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $transition_id := play_note($play_event, $play_velo, 0, - 1)
  change_vol($transition_id, - 200000, 0)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $current_trans_group)
  wait(1)
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
    end if
  else
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
    end if
  end if
  attach_zone(get_ui_id($wf_transition), get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx]
  %trans_zone_volume[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
  %trans_zone_pan[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_PAN)
  !trans_file_names[$trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $NI_FILE_NAME)
  note_off($transition_id)
  call update__gui__legato
  $sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%sus_release_time[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000.0) + 0.0)
  ~loc_23 := 0.0
  %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_23 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
  $keys := %range[0]
  while($keys <= %range[1]) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  call play_trans_sample
  call save__arrays

      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
    end if
  else
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
    end if
  end if
  attach_zone(get_ui_id($wf_transition), get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx]
  %trans_zone_volume[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
  %trans_zone_pan[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_PAN)
  !trans_file_names[$trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $NI_FILE_NAME)
  note_off($transition_id)
  call update__gui__legato
  $sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%sus_release_time[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000.0) + 0.0)
  ~loc_23 := 0.0
  %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_23 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
  $keys := %range[0]
  while($keys <= %range[1]) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  if($btn_mute = $TRUE)
    call play_trans_sample
  end if
  call save__arrays
  wait(($CLICK_INTERVAL * 1000) + 2000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - %clicktime[1]) > $CLICK_INTERVAL)
    set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    %clicktime[2] := $FALSE
  end if
end on
on ui_control($btn_element_button2)
  set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par($btn_element_button2, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par($btn_element_button2, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
  set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par($btn_element_button2, $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))
  set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, get_control_par($btn_element_button2, $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
  set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  $btn_listBrowserDC := $FALSE
  %clicktime[0] := get_ui_id($btn_element_button2)
  %clicktime[1] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  if(($element__idx # -1) and (%legatoList__element_numbers[$element__idx] = %legatoList__element_numbers[$scroll__up + 2]))
    $btn_element_button2 := $TRUE
  else
    %btn_elements_onoff[$scroll__up + 2] := get_control_par($btn_element_button2, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
  end if
  set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[26], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[$btn_element_button2 * 2])
  set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[38], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[$btn_element_button2 * 2])
  set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[62], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[$btn_element_button2 * 2])
  set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[2], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[$btn_element_button2 * 2])
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 11) 
    if($i # 2)
      set_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, $FALSE)
      set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
      set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
      set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
      set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 1)) 
    if($i # ($scroll__up + 2))
      %btn_elements_onoff[$i] := 0
    else
      if(get_control_par($btn_element_button2, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) = $TRUE)
        $element__idx := %legatoList__element_numbers[$i]
      else
        $element__idx := - 1
      end if
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    $play_event := lsb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
    $play_velo := msb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
  else
    $play_event := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)
    $play_velo := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_LOW_VELO)
  end if
  $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $mnu_rr := %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $transition_id := play_note($play_event, $play_velo, 0, - 1)
  change_vol($transition_id, - 200000, 0)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $current_trans_group)
  wait(1)
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
    end if
  else
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
    end if
  end if
  attach_zone(get_ui_id($wf_transition), get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx]

      set_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, $FALSE)
      set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
      set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
      set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
      set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 1)) 
    if($i # ($scroll__up + 4))
      %btn_elements_onoff[$i] := 0
    else
      if(get_control_par($btn_element_button4, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) = $TRUE)
        $element__idx := %legatoList__element_numbers[$i]
      else
        $element__idx := - 1
      end if
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    $play_event := lsb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
    $play_velo := msb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
  else
    $play_event := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)
    $play_velo := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_LOW_VELO)
  end if
  $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $mnu_rr := %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $transition_id := play_note($play_event, $play_velo, 0, - 1)
  change_vol($transition_id, - 200000, 0)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $current_trans_group)
  wait(1)
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
    end if
  else
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
    end if
  end if
  attach_zone(get_ui_id($wf_transition), get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx]
  %trans_zone_volume[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
  %trans_zone_pan[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_PAN)
  !trans_file_names[$trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $NI_FILE_NAME)
  note_off($transition_id)
  call update__gui__legato
  $sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%sus_release_time[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000.0) + 0.0)
  ~loc_23 := 0.0
  %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_23 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
  $keys := %range[0]
  while($keys <= %range[1]) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  if($btn_mute = $TRUE)
    call play_trans_sample
  end if
  call save__arrays
  wait(($CLICK_INTERVAL * 1000) + 2000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - %clicktime[1]) > $CLICK_INTERVAL)
    set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    %clicktime[2] := $FALSE
  end if
end on

  while($keys <= %range[1]) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  if($btn_mute = $TRUE)
    call play_trans_sample
  end if
  call save__arrays
  wait(($CLICK_INTERVAL * 1000) + 2000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - %clicktime[1]) > $CLICK_INTERVAL)
    set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    %clicktime[2] := $FALSE
  end if
end on
on ui_control($btn_element_button7)
  set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par($btn_element_button7, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par($btn_element_button7, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
  set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par($btn_element_button7, $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))
  set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, get_control_par($btn_element_button7, $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
  set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  $btn_listBrowserDC := $FALSE
  %clicktime[0] := get_ui_id($btn_element_button7)
  %clicktime[1] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  if(($element__idx # -1) and (%legatoList__element_numbers[$element__idx] = %legatoList__element_numbers[$scroll__up + 7]))
    $btn_element_button7 := $TRUE
  else
    %btn_elements_onoff[$scroll__up + 7] := get_control_par($btn_element_button7, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
  end if
  set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[31], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[$btn_element_button7 * 2])
  set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[43], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[$btn_element_button7 * 2])
  set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[67], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[$btn_element_button7 * 2])
  set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[7], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[$btn_element_button7 * 2])
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 11) 
    if($i # 7)
      set_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, $FALSE)
      set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
      set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
      set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
      set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 1)) 
    if($i # ($scroll__up + 7))
      %btn_elements_onoff[$i] := 0
    else
      if(get_control_par($btn_element_button7, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) = $TRUE)
        $element__idx := %legatoList__element_numbers[$i]
      else
        $element__idx := - 1
      end if
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    $play_event := lsb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
    $play_velo := msb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
  else
    $play_event := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)
    $play_velo := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_LOW_VELO)
  end if
  $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $mnu_rr := %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $transition_id := play_note($play_event, $play_velo, 0, - 1)
  change_vol($transition_id, - 200000, 0)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $current_trans_group)
  wait(1)
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
    end if
  else
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
    end if
  end if
  attach_zone(get_ui_id($wf_transition), get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx]
  %trans_zone_volume[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
  %trans_zone_pan[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_PAN)
  !trans_file_names[$trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $NI_FILE_NAME)
  note_off($transition_id)
  call update__gui__legato
  $sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%sus_release_time[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000.0) + 0.0)
  ~loc_23 := 0.0
  %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_23 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
  $keys := %range[0]
  while($keys <= %range[1]) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  if($btn_mute = $TRUE)
    call play_trans_sample
  end if
  call save__arrays
  wait(($CLICK_INTERVAL * 1000) + 2000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - %clicktime[1]) > $CLICK_INTERVAL)
    set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    %clicktime[2] := $FALSE
  end if
end on

  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx]
  %trans_zone_volume[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
  %trans_zone_pan[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_PAN)
  !trans_file_names[$trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $NI_FILE_NAME)
  note_off($transition_id)
  call update__gui__legato
  $sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%sus_release_time[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000.0) + 0.0)
  ~loc_23 := 0.0
  %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_23 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((~loc_23 * 1000.0) - 0.0) * 99.0) / (int_to_real($sample_length) - 0.0)) + 0.0), 31)))
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))
  $sli_waitSus := %trans_wait_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__waitSus
  $sli_fadeInSus := %sus_fadeIn_time[$trans_idx]
  call update__fadeInSus
  call reset__label_texts
  $keys := %range[0]
  while($keys <= %range[1]) 
    set_key_color($keys, $KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
    inc($keys)
  end while
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  set_key_color(%played_interval, $KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
  if($btn_mute = $TRUE)
    call play_trans_sample
  end if
  call save__arrays
  wait(($CLICK_INTERVAL * 1000) + 2000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - %clicktime[1]) > $CLICK_INTERVAL)
    set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    %clicktime[2] := $FALSE
  end if
end on
on ui_control($btn_element_button10)
  set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par($btn_element_button10, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
  set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par($btn_element_button10, $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
  set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par($btn_element_button10, $CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))
  set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, get_control_par($btn_element_button10, $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
  set_control_par($btn_listBrowserDC, $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
  $btn_listBrowserDC := $FALSE
  %clicktime[0] := get_ui_id($btn_element_button10)
  %clicktime[1] := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  if(($element__idx # -1) and (%legatoList__element_numbers[$element__idx] = %legatoList__element_numbers[$scroll__up + 10]))
    $btn_element_button10 := $TRUE
  else
    %btn_elements_onoff[$scroll__up + 10] := get_control_par($btn_element_button10, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
  end if
  set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[34], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[$btn_element_button10 * 2])
  set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[46], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[$btn_element_button10 * 2])
  set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[70], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[$btn_element_button10 * 2])
  set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[10], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[$btn_element_button10 * 2])
  $i := 0
  while($i <= 11) 
    if($i # 10)
      set_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, $FALSE)
      set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[24 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
      set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[36 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
      set_control_par(%_lbl_file_infos[60 + $i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
      set_control_par(!txt_element_marked[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, %_font__2pt7[get_control_par(%btn_element_button[$i], $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 1)) 
    if($i # ($scroll__up + 10))
      %btn_elements_onoff[$i] := 0
    else
      if(get_control_par($btn_element_button10, $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) = $TRUE)
        $element__idx := %legatoList__element_numbers[$i]
      else
        $element__idx := - 1
      end if
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    $play_event := lsb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
    $play_velo := msb(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx])
  else
    $play_event := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)
    $play_velo := get_zone_par(%legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx], $ZONE_PAR_LOW_VELO)
  end if
  $current_trans_group := $trans_group + %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $mnu_rr := %legatoList__trans_zone_groups[$element__idx]
  $transition_id := play_note($play_event, $play_velo, 0, - 1)
  change_vol($transition_id, - 200000, 0)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, $ALL_GROUPS)
  set_event_par_arr($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, $current_trans_group)
  wait(1)
  if(1 = $TRUE)
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs($trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
    end if
  else
    if(search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = -1)
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, - 1)
    else
      $trans_idx := search(%trans_zone_ids, get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
    end if
  end if
  attach_zone(get_ui_id($wf_transition), get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
  %trans_zone_ids[$trans_idx] := %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$element__idx]
  %trans_zone_volume[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
  %trans_zone_pan[$trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $ZONE_PAR_PAN)
  !trans_file_names[$trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par($transition_id, $EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), $NI_FILE_NAME)
  note_off($transition_id)
  call update__gui__legato
  $sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(%sus_release_time[$trans_idx]) - 0.0) * 1000000.0) / 1000.0) + 0.0)
  ~loc_23 := 0.0
  %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0)
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseSus), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, %sus_release_time[$trans_idx] & " ms")
  ~loc_23 := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_releaseSus)) - 0.0) * 1000.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0

  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_releaseCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_samplestartInd), $CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0.0)) / 99.0) + 0.0))

on ui_control($btn_scan)
  $btn_scan := $FALSE
  call scan__samples
  $loc_11 := 0
  $loc_13 := 0
  $loc_11 := 0
  while($loc_11 <= 1999) 
    %legatoList__element_numbers[$loc_11] := $loc_11
    !legatoList__trans_file_names[$loc_11] := !file_names_master[$loc_11]
    %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$loc_11] := %zone_ids_master[$loc_11]
    %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_11] := 0
    !legatoList__intervals[$loc_11] := ""
    !legatoList__comments[$loc_11] := ""
    inc($loc_11)
  end while
  $loc_11 := 0
  while($loc_11 <= ($NUM_TRANS_SAMPLES_PLAYED - 1)) 
    $loc_13 := search(%zone_ids_master, %trans_zone_ids[$loc_11])
    if($loc_13 # -1)
      %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_13] := %marked_samples[$loc_11]
      !legatoList__intervals[$loc_13] := !intervals[$loc_11]
      !legatoList__comments[$loc_13] := !sample_comments[$loc_11]
    end if
    inc($loc_11)
  end while
  $loc_11 := 0
  $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD := $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS
  $NUM_PRESETS := search(%zone_ids_master, - 1)
  $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS := $NUM_PRESETS
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_presetcount), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS & "/" & $NUM_PRESETS)
  if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD # $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
    $loc_11 := 0
    while($loc_11 <= (num_elements(%legatoList__end_of_list) - 1)) 
      %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := - 1
      if($loc_11 < $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
        %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := 1
      end if
      inc($loc_11)
    end while
  end if
  $scroll__up := real_to_int((((~scroll__realup - 0.0) * (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD - 12) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
  call update__preset_button_focus
  call update__scrollbar
  call update__scrollarea
  if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS > 12)
    $sli_scrollbar := 1000000 - ((1000000 / ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12)) * $scroll__up)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_MOUSE_BEHAVIOUR, - (4248 + (2 * ($NUM_PRESETS - $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS))))
    $handle_size := real_to_int(round(int_to_real(245) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS) / int_to_real(12))))
    if($handle_size < 30)
      $handle_size := 30
    end if
  else
    $sli_scrollbar := 1000000
    $handle_size := 245
  end if
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, $handle_size)
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + ((245 - $handle_size) - (($sli_scrollbar * (245 - $handle_size)) / 1000000)))
end on
on ui_control($btn_vibratoSettings)
  $btn_home := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_home), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_reverb), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_eq), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  $btn_settings := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_settings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  $btn_legatoSettings := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_dataSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_waveform), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_sustainSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_resetWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_forallWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  call reset__label_texts
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  $btn_legatoList := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_legatoList), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoList])
  if(- sh_right(abs(%development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
    $loc_13 := 0
    $loc_12 := 0
    $loc_13 := 0
    while($loc_13 <= 1999) 
      %legatoList__element_numbers[$loc_13] := $loc_13
      !legatoList__trans_file_names[$loc_13] := !file_names_master[$loc_13]
      %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$loc_13] := %zone_ids_master[$loc_13]
      %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_13] := 0
      !legatoList__intervals[$loc_13] := ""
      !legatoList__comments[$loc_13] := ""
      inc($loc_13)
    end while
    $loc_13 := 0
    while($loc_13 <= ($NUM_TRANS_SAMPLES_PLAYED - 1)) 
      $loc_12 := search(%zone_ids_master, %trans_zone_ids[$loc_13])
      if($loc_12 # -1)
        %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_12] := %marked_samples[$loc_13]
        !legatoList__intervals[$loc_12] := !intervals[$loc_13]
        !legatoList__comments[$loc_12] := !sample_comments[$loc_13]
      end if
      inc($loc_13)
    end while
    $loc_11 := 0
    $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD := $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS
    $NUM_PRESETS := search(%zone_ids_master, - 1)
    $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS := $NUM_PRESETS
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_presetcount), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS & "/" & $NUM_PRESETS)
    if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD # $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
      $loc_11 := 0
      while($loc_11 <= (num_elements(%legatoList__end_of_list) - 1)) 
        %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := - 1
        if($loc_11 < $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
          %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := 1
        end if
        inc($loc_11)
      end while
    end if
    $scroll__up := real_to_int((((~scroll__realup - 0.0) * (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD - 12) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
    call update__preset_button_focus
    call update__scrollbar
    call update__scrollarea
    if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS > 12)
      $sli_scrollbar := 1000000 - ((1000000 / ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12)) * $scroll__up)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_MOUSE_BEHAVIOUR, - (4248 + (2 * ($NUM_PRESETS - $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS))))
      $handle_size := real_to_int(round(int_to_real(245) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS) / int_to_real(12))))
      if($handle_size < 30)
        $handle_size := 30
      end if
    else
      $sli_scrollbar := 1000000
      $handle_size := 245
    end if
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, $handle_size)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + ((245 - $handle_size) - (($sli_scrollbar * (245 - $handle_size)) / 1000000)))
  end if
  $btn_vibratoSettings := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  $btn_vibratoSettings := $TRUE
  $btn_vibratoSettings := $btn_vibratoSettings
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_vibratoSettings])
end on

on ui_control($sli_envRateCurve)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0], get_ui_id($sli_envRateCurve), %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "ENV_AHDSR"), - 1)
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_rate__curve := $sli_envRateCurve
  ~tbl_rate__attack_point := pow(10.0, (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)) + ((((int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.510000000000000) - 0.0) / (int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0.0)) * ((log(0.056000000000000) / log(10.0)) - (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)))))
  $tbl_rate__release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.750000000000000)
  ~tbl_rate__attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_envRateAttack)) - 0.0) * (~tbl_rate__attack_point - 1.500000000000000)) / 1000000.0) + 1.500000000000000
  $tbl_rate__hold := (($sli_envRateHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.150000000000000) - 0)) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_envRateDecay)) - 0.0) * 14200.0) / 1000000.0) + 800.0
  $tbl_rate__sustain := (($sli_envRateSustain - 0) * 1000) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0.0) * 39200.0) / 1000000.0) + 800.0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := real_to_int(exp(~tbl_rate__attack * int_to_real($i)))
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1.0 / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.0) * 10.990000000000000) / 14200.0) + 0.010000000000000))) * ~tbl_rate__decay) - ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.0) * 200.0) / 14200.0) + 0.0))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := (((%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] - 0) * (1000 - $tbl_rate__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_rate__sustain
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1.0 / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.0) * 4.990000000000000) / 14200.0) + 0.010000000000000))) * ~tbl_rate__release) - ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.0) * 300.0) / 14200.0) + 0.0))
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_rate__attack_idx := search(%tbl_rate__expCurve, 1000)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__linCurve[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real($i) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($tbl_rate__attack_idx) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
    %tbl_rate__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[((($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right(($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31))) - ($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_rate__curve < 500000)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.0) * -1.0) / 500000.0) + 1.0)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.0) * 1.0) / 500000.0) + 0.0))
    else
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.0) * -1.0) / 500000.0) + 1.0)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__logCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.0) * 1.0) / 500000.0) + 0.0))
    end if
    if($i > ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold))
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] - 0) * (real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$tbl_rate__release_idx]) - 0)) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_rate__release_idx)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_rate__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= ($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate1[$i] := (((((real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.880000000000000) - 0)) / 1000
    %tbl_rate2[$i] := %tbl_rate1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envRateCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0], %vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR"), -1) & " " & !ADHSR_UNITS[0])
  if(0 = 4)
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envRateCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, ($sli_envRateCurve / 10000) & " %")
  end if
  $last_time_envRateCurve := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_envRateCurve) > 795)
    set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_envRateCurve), !envRateNames[0])
  end if
end on

  end while
  $tbl_rate__curve := $sli_envRateCurve
  ~tbl_rate__attack_point := pow(10.0, (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)) + ((((int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.510000000000000) - 0.0) / (int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0.0)) * ((log(0.056000000000000) / log(10.0)) - (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)))))
  $tbl_rate__release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.750000000000000)
  ~tbl_rate__attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_envRateAttack)) - 0.0) * (~tbl_rate__attack_point - 1.500000000000000)) / 1000000.0) + 1.500000000000000
  $tbl_rate__hold := (($sli_envRateHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.150000000000000) - 0)) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_envRateDecay)) - 0.0) * 14200.0) / 1000000.0) + 800.0
  $tbl_rate__sustain := (($sli_envRateSustain - 0) * 1000) / 1000000
  ~tbl_rate__release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0.0) * 39200.0) / 1000000.0) + 800.0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := real_to_int(exp(~tbl_rate__attack * int_to_real($i)))
    %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1.0 / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.0) * 10.990000000000000) / 14200.0) + 0.010000000000000))) * ~tbl_rate__decay) - ((((~tbl_rate__decay - 800.0) * 200.0) / 14200.0) + 0.0))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] := (((%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i] - 0) * (1000 - $tbl_rate__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_rate__sustain
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1.0 / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.0) * 4.990000000000000) / 14200.0) + 0.010000000000000))) * ~tbl_rate__release) - ((((~tbl_rate__release - 800.0) * 300.0) / 14200.0) + 0.0))
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_rate__attack_idx := search(%tbl_rate__expCurve, 1000)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__linCurve[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real($i) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($tbl_rate__attack_idx) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
    %tbl_rate__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_rate__expCurve[((($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right(($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31))) - ($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_rate__curve < 500000)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__expCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.0) * -1.0) / 500000.0) + 1.0)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 0.0) * 1.0) / 500000.0) + 0.0))
    else
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.0) * -1.0) / 500000.0) + 1.0)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_rate__logCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_rate__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_rate__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_rate__curve, 31))) - 500000.0) * 1.0) / 500000.0) + 0.0))
    end if
    if($i > ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold))
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__decayCurve[$i - ($tbl_rate__attack_idx + $tbl_rate__hold)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i] - 0) * (real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$tbl_rate__release_idx]) - 0)) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_rate__release_idx)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_rate__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= ($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate1[$i] := (((((real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.880000000000000) - 0)) / 1000
    %tbl_rate2[$i] := %tbl_rate1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envRateHold), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[2], %vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR"), -1) & " " & !ADHSR_UNITS[2])
  if(2 = 4)
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envRateHold), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, ($sli_envRateHold / 10000) & " %")
  end if
  $last_time_envRateHold := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_envRateHold) > 795)
    set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_envRateHold), !envRateNames[2])
  end if
end on

  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_rate__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_rate__release_idx)
      ?tbl_rate__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_rate__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_rate__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= ($tbl_rate__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
    %tbl_rate1[$i] := (((((real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_rate__env_array[$i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.880000000000000) - 0)) / 1000
    %tbl_rate2[$i] := %tbl_rate1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envRateSustain), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[4], %vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR"), -1) & " " & !ADHSR_UNITS[4])
  if(4 = 4)
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envRateSustain), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, ($sli_envRateSustain / 10000) & " %")
  end if
  $last_time_envRateSustain := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_envRateSustain) > 795)
    set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_envRateSustain), !envRateNames[4])
  end if
end on

on ui_control($sli_envIntCurve)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (search(%vibrato_groups, -1) - 1)) 
    set_engine_par(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0], get_ui_id($sli_envIntCurve), %vibrato_groups[$i], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[$i], "ENV_AHDSR2"), - 1)
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_int__curve := $sli_envIntCurve
  ~tbl_int__attack_point := pow(10.0, (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)) + ((((int_to_real($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.510000000000000) - 0.0) / (int_to_real($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0.0)) * ((log(0.056000000000000) / log(10.0)) - (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)))))
  $tbl_int__release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.750000000000000)
  ~tbl_int__attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_envIntAttack)) - 0.0) * (~tbl_int__attack_point - 1.500000000000000)) / 1000000.0) + 1.500000000000000
  $tbl_int__hold := (($sli_envIntHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.150000000000000) - 0)) / 1000000
  ~tbl_int__decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_envIntDecay)) - 0.0) * 14200.0) / 1000000.0) + 800.0
  $tbl_int__sustain := (($sli_envIntSustain - 0) * 1000) / 1000000
  ~tbl_int__release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0.0) * 39200.0) / 1000000.0) + 800.0
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__expCurve[$i] := real_to_int(exp(~tbl_int__attack * int_to_real($i)))
    %tbl_int__expCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_int__expCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__expCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_int__expCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1.0 / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_int__decay - 800.0) * 10.990000000000000) / 14200.0) + 0.010000000000000))) * ~tbl_int__decay) - ((((~tbl_int__decay - 800.0) * 200.0) / 14200.0) + 0.0))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := (((%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] - 0) * (1000 - $tbl_int__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_int__sustain
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1.0 / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_int__release - 800.0) * 4.990000000000000) / 14200.0) + 0.010000000000000))) * ~tbl_int__release) - ((((~tbl_int__release - 800.0) * 300.0) / 14200.0) + 0.0))
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_int__attack_idx := search(%tbl_int__expCurve, 1000)
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__linCurve[$i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real($i) - 0.0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($tbl_int__attack_idx) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
    %tbl_int__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[((($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right(($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31))) - ($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_int__curve < 500000)
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_int__expCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 0.0) * -1.0) / 500000.0) + 1.0)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_int__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 0.0) * 1.0) / 500000.0) + 0.0))
    else
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_int__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 500000.0) * -1.0) / 500000.0) + 1.0)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_int__logCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 500000.0) * 1.0) / 500000.0) + 0.0))
    end if
    if($i > ($tbl_int__attack_idx + $tbl_int__hold))
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i - ($tbl_int__attack_idx + $tbl_int__hold)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] - 0) * (real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$tbl_int__release_idx]) - 0)) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_int__release_idx)
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_int__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= ($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
    %tbl_int1[$i] := (((((real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.880000000000000) - 0)) / 1000
    %tbl_int2[$i] := %tbl_int1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envIntCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0], %vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR2"), -1) & " " & !ADHSR_UNITS[0])
  if(0 = 4)
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envIntCurve), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, ($sli_envIntCurve / 10000) & " %")
  end if

  wait(800000)

    %tbl_int__logCurve[$i] := 1000 - %tbl_int__expCurve[((($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i) * (1 + (sh_right($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i), 31) .or. sh_right(($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i) - 0, 31))) - ($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - ($tbl_int__attack_idx - $i), 31))]
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($tbl_int__curve < 500000)
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_int__expCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 0.0) * -1.0) / 500000.0) + 1.0)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_int__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 0.0) * 1.0) / 500000.0) + 0.0))
    else
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := (int_to_real(%tbl_int__linCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 500000.0) * -1.0) / 500000.0) + 1.0)) + (int_to_real(%tbl_int__logCurve[$i]) * ((((int_to_real((($tbl_int__curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31) .or. sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right($tbl_int__curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - $tbl_int__curve, 31))) - 500000.0) * 1.0) / 500000.0) + 0.0))
    end if
    if($i > ($tbl_int__attack_idx + $tbl_int__hold))
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i - ($tbl_int__attack_idx + $tbl_int__hold)])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] - 0) * (real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$tbl_int__release_idx]) - 0)) / 1000
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= (num_elements(?tbl_int__env_array) - 1)) 
    if($i > $tbl_int__release_idx)
      ?tbl_int__env_array[$i] := int_to_real(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i - $tbl_int__release_idx])
    end if
    inc($i)
  end while
  $i := 0
  while($i <= ($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
    %tbl_int1[$i] := (((((real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(?tbl_int__env_array[$i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.880000000000000) - 0)) / 1000
    %tbl_int2[$i] := %tbl_int1[$i]
    inc($i)
  end while
  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envIntHold), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(%ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[2], %vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR2"), -1) & " " & !ADHSR_UNITS[2])
  if(2 = 4)
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_envIntHold), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, ($sli_envIntHold / 10000) & " %")
  end if

  wait(800000)

    set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_envIntHold), !envRateNames[2])
  end if
end on

    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_int__curve := $sli_envIntCurve
  ~tbl_int__attack_point := pow(10.0, (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)) + ((((int_to_real($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.510000000000000) - 0.0) / (int_to_real($tbl_int__NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0.0)) * ((log(0.056000000000000) / log(10.0)) - (log(1.500000000000000) / log(10.0)))))

    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i], 31))
    %tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] := (((%tbl_int__decayCurve[$i] - 0) * (1000 - $tbl_int__sustain)) / 1000) + $tbl_int__sustain
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := real_to_int(((1.0 / (int_to_real($i) + ((((~tbl_int__release - 800.0) * 4.990000000000000) / 14200.0) + 0.010000000000000))) * ~tbl_int__release) - ((((~tbl_int__release - 800.0) * 300.0) / 14200.0) + 0.0))
    %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] := ((%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31) .or. sh_right(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(%tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - %tbl_int__releaseCurve[$i], 31))
    inc($i)
  end while
  $tbl_int__attack_idx := search(%tbl_int__expCurve, 1000)

  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_lfoFreq), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp($ENGINE_PAR_INTMOD_FREQUENCY, %vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(%vibrato_groups[0], "LFO_MULTI D"), -1) & " Hz")
  $last_time_lfoFreq := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_lfoFreq) > 795)
    set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_lfoFreq), !lfoNames[0])
  end if
end on
on ui_control($sli_lfoRand)

  set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_lfoRand), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, ($sli_lfoRand / 10000) & " %")
  $last_time_lfoRand := $ENGINE_UPTIME
  wait(800000)
  if(($ENGINE_UPTIME - $last_time_lfoRand) > 795)
    set_text(get_ui_id($lbl_lfoRand), !lfoNames[1])
  end if
end on
