on ui_control($btn_prevPreset)
  $btn_prevPreset := $FALSE
  $mnu_preset := (($mnu_preset - 1) + $presetCount) mod $presetCount
  call update__preset__menu
  if($presetCount # 0)
    call load__preset
  end if
end on
on ui_control($btn_nextPreset)
  $btn_nextPreset := $FALSE
  $mnu_preset := ($mnu_preset + 1) mod $presetCount
  call update__preset__menu
  if($presetCount # 0)
    call load__preset
  end if
end on
on ui_control($btn_savePreset)
  $btn_savePreset := $FALSE
  call save__preset
end on
on ui_control($btn_deletePreset)
  $btn_deletePreset := $FALSE
  call delete__preset
end on
on ui_control($mouse_nka)
  if($NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE = $NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_DROP)
    wait_async(load_array_str(%vibrato_preset, !NI_DND_ITEMS_ARRAY[0]))
    call load__array
  end if
end on
on ui_control($btn_scanPresets)
  if($preset_scan = $FALSE)
    $preset_scan := $TRUE
    $i := 0
    while($i <= (num_elements(%vibPresetCount) - 1)) 
      %vibPresetCount[$i] := 0
      !vibPresetNames[$i] := ""
      inc($i)
    end while
    $lib__i := 0
    while($lib__i <= (num_elements(%vibrato_preset2) - 1)) 
      %vibrato_preset2[$lib__i] := 0
      inc($lib__i)
    end while
    $lib__i := 0
    while($lib__i <= (num_elements(%vibrato_preset) - 1)) 
      %vibrato_preset[$lib__i] := 0
      inc($lib__i)
    end while
    $presetCount := 0
    fs_navigate(get_ui_id($file_browser), 1)
  end if
end on
on ui_control($file_browser)
  message("File Browser triggered")
  wait_async(load_array_str(%vibrato_preset, fs_get_filename(get_ui_id($file_browser), 2)))
  if(($preset_scan = $TRUE) and (%vibrato_preset[$preset_idx__DELETED] # -420))
    if(%vibrato_preset[$preset_idx__DELETED] = 0)
      if(not array_equal(%vibrato_preset, %vibrato_preset2))
        !vibPresetNames[$presetCount] := fs_get_filename(get_ui_id($file_browser), 0)
        %vibPresetCount[$presetCount] := 1
        inc($presetCount)
      end if
      $lib__i := 0
      while($lib__i <= (num_elements(%vibrato_preset) - 1)) 
        %vibrato_preset[$lib__i] := 0
        inc($lib__i)
      end while
    else
      if(((%vibrato_preset[$preset_idx__DELETED] = 0) or (%vibrato_preset[$preset_idx__DELETED] = 1)) and (get_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_scanPresets), $CONTROL_PAR_KEY_ALT) = $TRUE))
        message("Scanning for deleted")
        if(not array_equal(%vibrato_preset, %vibrato_preset2))
          !vibPresetNames[$presetCount] := fs_get_filename(get_ui_id($file_browser), 0)
          %vibPresetCount[$presetCount] := 1
          inc($presetCount)
          %vibrato_preset[$preset_idx__DELETED] := $FALSE
          save_array_str(%vibrato_preset, fs_get_filename(get_ui_id($file_browser), 2))
        end if
        $lib__i := 0
        while($lib__i <= (num_elements(%vibrato_preset) - 1)) 
          %vibrato_preset[$lib__i] := 0
          inc($lib__i)
        end while
      end if
    end if
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_scanPresets), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, $TRUE)
    fs_navigate(get_ui_id($file_browser), 1)
  else
    message("The end")
    call save__resource_arrays
    call get__presetCount
    $preset_scan := $FALSE
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_scanPresets), $CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, $FALSE)
    call update__preset__menu
    call load__preset
  end if
end on
on ui_control($mnu_preset)
  call update__preset__menu
  call load__preset
end on
on async_complete
  if($NI_ASYNC_ID = $save_id)
    if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS = $TRUE)
      $save_id := - 1
    else
      if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS = $FALSE)
        $save_id := 0
      end if
    end if
  end if
  if($NI_ASYNC_ID = $load_id)
    if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS = $TRUE)
      $load_id := - 1
    else
      if($NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS = $FALSE)
        $load_id := 0
      end if
    end if
  end if
end on
on ui_control($btn_home)
  $btn_home := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_home), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_reverb), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_eq), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  $btn_settings := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_settings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  $btn_legatoSettings := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_dataSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_waveform), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_sustainSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_resetWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_forallWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  call reset__label_texts
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
  $btn_legatoList := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_legatoList), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoList])
  if(- sh_right(abs(%development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
    $loc_13 := 0
    $loc_12 := 0
    $loc_13 := 0
    while($loc_13 <= 1999) 
      %legatoList__element_numbers[$loc_13] := $loc_13
      !legatoList__trans_file_names[$loc_13] := !file_names_master[$loc_13]
      %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$loc_13] := %zone_ids_master[$loc_13]
      %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_13] := 0
      !legatoList__intervals[$loc_13] := ""
      !legatoList__comments[$loc_13] := ""
      inc($loc_13)
    end while
    $loc_13 := 0
    while($loc_13 <= ($NUM_TRANS_SAMPLES_PLAYED - 1)) 
      $loc_12 := search(%zone_ids_master, %trans_zone_ids[$loc_13])
      if($loc_12 # -1)
        %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_12] := %marked_samples[$loc_13]
        !legatoList__intervals[$loc_12] := !intervals[$loc_13]
        !legatoList__comments[$loc_12] := !sample_comments[$loc_13]
      end if
      inc($loc_13)
    end while
    $loc_11 := 0
    $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD := $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS
    $NUM_PRESETS := search(%zone_ids_master, - 1)
    $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS := $NUM_PRESETS
    set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_presetcount), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS & "/" & $NUM_PRESETS)
    if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD # $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
      $loc_11 := 0
      while($loc_11 <= (num_elements(%legatoList__end_of_list) - 1)) 
        %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := - 1
        if($loc_11 < $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
          %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := 1
        end if
        inc($loc_11)
      end while
    end if
    $scroll__up := real_to_int((((~scroll__realup - 0.0) * (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD - 12) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
    call update__preset_button_focus
    call update__scrollbar
    call update__scrollarea
    if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS > 12)
      $sli_scrollbar := 1000000 - ((1000000 / ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12)) * $scroll__up)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_MOUSE_BEHAVIOUR, - (4248 + (2 * ($NUM_PRESETS - $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS))))
      $handle_size := real_to_int(round(int_to_real(245) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS) / int_to_real(12))))
      if($handle_size < 30)
        $handle_size := 30
      end if
    else
      $sli_scrollbar := 1000000
      $handle_size := 245
    end if
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, $handle_size)
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + ((245 - $handle_size) - (($sli_scrollbar * (245 - $handle_size)) / 1000000)))
  end if
  $btn_vibratoSettings := $FALSE
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
  $btn_home := $TRUE
  $btn_home := $btn_home
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_home), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_home])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_reverb), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_home])
  set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_eq), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
end on
on ui_control($sli_dynamics)
  set_controller(103, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_dynamics)) - 0.0) * 127.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0))
end on

  set_controller(111, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id($sli_expression)) - 0.0) * 127.0) / 1000000.0) + 0.0))
end on

  end if

on ui_control($btn_settings)
  if($btn_settings = $TRUE)
    $btn_home := $FALSE
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_home), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_reverb), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_eq), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    $btn_settings := $FALSE
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_settings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    $btn_legatoSettings := $FALSE
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_dataSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_waveform), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_sustainSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_resetWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_forallWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    call reset__label_texts
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
    $btn_legatoList := $FALSE
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_legatoList), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoList])
    if(- sh_right(abs(%development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
      $loc_13 := 0
      $loc_12 := 0
      $loc_13 := 0
      while($loc_13 <= 1999) 
        %legatoList__element_numbers[$loc_13] := $loc_13
        !legatoList__trans_file_names[$loc_13] := !file_names_master[$loc_13]
        %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$loc_13] := %zone_ids_master[$loc_13]
        %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_13] := 0
        !legatoList__intervals[$loc_13] := ""
        !legatoList__comments[$loc_13] := ""
        inc($loc_13)
      end while
      $loc_13 := 0
      while($loc_13 <= ($NUM_TRANS_SAMPLES_PLAYED - 1)) 
        $loc_12 := search(%zone_ids_master, %trans_zone_ids[$loc_13])
        if($loc_12 # -1)
          %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_12] := %marked_samples[$loc_13]
          !legatoList__intervals[$loc_12] := !intervals[$loc_13]
          !legatoList__comments[$loc_12] := !sample_comments[$loc_13]
        end if
        inc($loc_13)
      end while
      $loc_11 := 0
      $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD := $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS
      $NUM_PRESETS := search(%zone_ids_master, - 1)
      $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS := $NUM_PRESETS
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_presetcount), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS & "/" & $NUM_PRESETS)
      if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD # $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
        $loc_11 := 0
        while($loc_11 <= (num_elements(%legatoList__end_of_list) - 1)) 
          %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := - 1
          if($loc_11 < $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
            %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := 1
          end if
          inc($loc_11)
        end while
      end if
      $scroll__up := real_to_int((((~scroll__realup - 0.0) * (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD - 12) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
      call update__preset_button_focus
      call update__scrollbar
      call update__scrollarea
      if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS > 12)
        $sli_scrollbar := 1000000 - ((1000000 / ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12)) * $scroll__up)
        set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_MOUSE_BEHAVIOUR, - (4248 + (2 * ($NUM_PRESETS - $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS))))
        $handle_size := real_to_int(round(int_to_real(245) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS) / int_to_real(12))))
        if($handle_size < 30)
          $handle_size := 30
        end if
      else
        $sli_scrollbar := 1000000
        $handle_size := 245
      end if
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, $handle_size)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + ((245 - $handle_size) - (($sli_scrollbar * (245 - $handle_size)) / 1000000)))
    end if
    $btn_vibratoSettings := $FALSE
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    $btn_settings := $TRUE
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_settings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$TRUE])
  else
    $btn_home := $FALSE
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_home), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_reverb), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_eq), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
    $btn_settings := $FALSE
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_settings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    $btn_legatoSettings := $FALSE
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_dataSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_waveform), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_sustainSettings), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_resetWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs($FALSE) - 1, 31))])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_forallWindow), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_checkButtons), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    call reset__label_texts
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_reset), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($btn_forall), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoSettings])
    $btn_legatoList := $FALSE
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_legatoList), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$btn_legatoList])
    if(- sh_right(abs(%development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
      $loc_13 := 0
      $loc_12 := 0
      $loc_13 := 0
      while($loc_13 <= 1999) 
        %legatoList__element_numbers[$loc_13] := $loc_13
        !legatoList__trans_file_names[$loc_13] := !file_names_master[$loc_13]
        %legatoList__trans_zone_ids[$loc_13] := %zone_ids_master[$loc_13]
        %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_13] := 0
        !legatoList__intervals[$loc_13] := ""
        !legatoList__comments[$loc_13] := ""
        inc($loc_13)
      end while
      $loc_13 := 0
      while($loc_13 <= ($NUM_TRANS_SAMPLES_PLAYED - 1)) 
        $loc_12 := search(%zone_ids_master, %trans_zone_ids[$loc_13])
        if($loc_12 # -1)
          %legatoList__marked_elements[$loc_12] := %marked_samples[$loc_13]
          !legatoList__intervals[$loc_12] := !intervals[$loc_13]
          !legatoList__comments[$loc_12] := !sample_comments[$loc_13]
        end if
        inc($loc_13)
      end while
      $loc_11 := 0
      $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD := $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS
      $NUM_PRESETS := search(%zone_ids_master, - 1)
      $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS := $NUM_PRESETS
      set_control_par_str(get_ui_id($lbl_presetcount), $CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS & "/" & $NUM_PRESETS)
      if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD # $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
        $loc_11 := 0
        while($loc_11 <= (num_elements(%legatoList__end_of_list) - 1)) 
          %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := - 1
          if($loc_11 < $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
            %legatoList__end_of_list[$loc_11] := 1
          end if
          inc($loc_11)
        end while
      end if
      $scroll__up := real_to_int((((~scroll__realup - 0.0) * (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - 0.0)) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD - 12) - 0.0)) + 0.0)
      call update__preset_button_focus
      call update__scrollbar
      call update__scrollarea
      if($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS > 12)
        $sli_scrollbar := 1000000 - ((1000000 / ($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12)) * $scroll__up)
        set_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_MOUSE_BEHAVIOUR, - (4248 + (2 * ($NUM_PRESETS - $NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS))))
        $handle_size := real_to_int(round(int_to_real(245) / (int_to_real($NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS) / int_to_real(12))))
        if($handle_size < 30)
          $handle_size := 30
        end if
      else
        $sli_scrollbar := 1000000
        $handle_size := 245
      end if
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, $handle_size)
      set_control_par(get_ui_id($lbl_scrollhandle), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id($sli_scrollbar), $CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + ((245 - $handle_size) - (($sli_scrollbar * (245 - $handle_size)) / 1000000)))
    end if
    $btn_vibratoSettings := $FALSE
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_vibrato), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$FALSE])
    $btn_home := $TRUE
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_home), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$TRUE])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_reverb), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, %hide_state[$TRUE])
    set_control_par(get_ui_id($UI_eq), $CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, $HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
  end if
end on
